### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Infraestrutura Auto-Escalável

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-infra/
├── kubernetes/
│   ├── namespaces/
│   ├── deployments/
│   ├── services/
│   ├── configmaps/
│   ├── secrets/
│   ├── hpa/

├── terraform/

│   ├── variables.tf
│   └── outputs.tf
├── monitoring/
│   ├── prometheus/
│   ├── grafana/
│   ├── loki/
│   └── alertmanager/
├── scripts/
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   └── backup.sh
├── docker/
│   └── Dockerfile
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
├── docs/
│   └── runbooks/
└── index.html
```

## 1. Kubernetes Manifests (K8s)

### 1.1 Namespace Configuration
```yaml
# kubernetes/namespaces/diyapp-namespace.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: diyapp-v11
  labels:
    name: diyapp-v11
    environment: production
    managed-by: terraform
```

### 1.2 Deployment com Health Checks e Auto-Scaling
```yaml
# kubernetes/deployments/diyapp-api.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp-v11
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    version: v11
    component: backend
spec:
  replicas: 3
  revisionHistoryLimit: 10
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-api
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-api
        version: v11
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "9100"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: diyapp-service-account
      containers:
      - name: diyapp-api
        image: diyapp/api:v11.0.0
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
          protocol: TCP
        - containerPort: 9100
          name: metrics
          protocol: TCP
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: LOG_LEVEL
          value: "info"
        - name: POD_NAME
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.name
        - name: POD_NAMESPACE
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.namespace
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/live
            port: 8080
            httpHeaders:
            - name: X-Health-Check
              value: "k8s-probe"
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          successThreshold: 1
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/ready
            port: 8080
            httpHeaders:
            - name: X-Health-Check
              value: "k8s-probe"
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          successThreshold: 1
          failureThreshold: 3
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/startup
            port: 8080
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 10
          failureThreshold: 30
        lifecycle:
          preStop:
            exec:
              command: ["/bin/sh", "-c", "sleep 30"]
        volumeMounts:
        - name: config-volume
          mountPath: /app/config
        - name: logs-volume
          mountPath: /var/log/diyapp
      - name: node-exporter
        image: prom/node-exporter:v1.5.0
        ports:
        - containerPort: 9100
          name: metrics
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "32Mi"
            cpu: "50m"
          limits:
            memory: "64Mi"
            cpu: "100m"
      volumes:
      - name: config-volume
        configMap:
          name: diyapp-config
      - name: logs-volume
        emptyDir: {}
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - weight: 100
            podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - diyapp-api
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
      tolerations:
      - key: "node.kubernetes.io/unreachable"
        operator: "Exists"
        effect: "NoExecute"
        tolerationSeconds: 300
      - key: "node.kubernetes.io/not-ready"
        operator: "Exists"
        effect: "NoExecute"
        tolerationSeconds: 300
```

### 1.3 Horizontal Pod Autoscaler
```yaml
# kubernetes/hpa/diyapp-api-hpa.yaml
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-hpa
  namespace: diyapp-v11
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: diyapp-api
  minReplicas: 3
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 70
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 80
  - type: Pods
    pods:
      metric:
        name: http_requests_per_second
      target:
        type: AverageValue
        averageValue: 100
  behavior:
    scaleUp:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 60
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 100
        periodSeconds: 60
      - type: Pods
        value: 4
        periodSeconds: 60
      selectPolicy: Max
    scaleDown:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 300
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 10
        periodSeconds: 60
      - type: Pods
        value: 2
        periodSeconds: 60
      selectPolicy: Min
```

### 1.4 Service Configuration
```yaml
# kubernetes/services/diyapp-api-service.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-service
  namespace: diyapp-v11
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    service: api
  annotations:
    prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
    prometheus.io/port: "9100"
spec:
  selector:
    app: diyapp-api
  ports:
  - name: http
    port: 80
    targetPort: 8080
    protocol: TCP
  - name: metrics
    port: 9100
    targetPort: 9100
    protocol: TCP
  type: ClusterIP
  sessionAffinity: None
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-headless
  namespace: diyapp-v11
spec:
  clusterIP: None
  selector:
    app: diyapp-api
  ports:
  - port: 8080
    name: http
```

### 1.5 Ingress com Health Checks
```yaml
# kubernetes/ingress/diyapp-ingress.yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: diyapp-ingress
  namespace: diyapp-v11
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: "nginx"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/force-ssl-redirect: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-body-size: "50m"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-read-timeout: "300"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-send-timeout: "300"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/configuration-snippet: |
      more_set_headers "X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff";
      more_set_headers "X-Frame-Options: DENY";
      more_set_headers "X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block";
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/health-check: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/health-check-path: "/health"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/health-check-interval: "30s"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/health-check-timeout: "5s"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/health-check-healthy-threshold: "2"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/health-check-unhealthy-threshold: "3"
spec:
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - api.diyapp.com
    secretName: diyapp-tls
  rules:
  - host: api.diyapp.com
    http:
      paths:
      - path: /
        pathType: Prefix
        backend:
          service:
            name: diyapp-api-service
            port:
              number: 80
```

### 1.6 ConfigMaps para Configuração
```yaml
# kubernetes/configmaps/diyapp-config.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: diyapp-config
  namespace: diyapp-v11
data:
  app.config.json: |
    {
      "server": {
        "port": 8080,
        "host": "0.0.0.0",
        "timeout": 30000
      },
      "logging": {
        "level": "info",
        "format": "json",
        "output": "stdout"
      },
      "database": {
        "maxConnections": 20,
        "idleTimeout": 30000,
        "connectionTimeout": 2000
      },
      "rateLimiting": {
        "enabled": true,
        "windowMs": 60000,
        "maxRequests": 100
      },
      "healthCheck": {
        "interval": 30000,
        "timeout": 5000,
        "threshold": 3
      }
    }
  prometheus.yml: |
    global:
      scrape_interval: 15s
      evaluation_interval: 15s
    
    scrape_configs:
      - job_name: 'diyapp-api'
        kubernetes_sd_configs:
          - role: pod
        relabel_configs:
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_app]
            regex: diyapp-api
            action: keep
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_container_port_number]
            regex: 9100
            action: keep
```

## 2. Terraform para Provisionamento

```hcl
# terraform/main.tf
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.3.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 4.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.16"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.8"
    }
  }
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "v11/production/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "SRE"
    }
  }
}

# EKS Cluster
module "eks" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/eks/aws"
  version = "~> 19.0"

  cluster_name    = "diyapp-v11-cluster"
  cluster_version = "1.27"

  vpc_id     = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = module.vpc.private_subnets

  cluster_endpoint_public_access = true

  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    diyapp = {
      min_size     = 3
      max_size     = 10
      desired_size = 3

      instance_types = ["t3.medium"]
      capacity_type  = "SPOT"

      update_config = {
        max_unavailable_percentage = 33
      }

      labels = {
        Environment = var.environment
        NodeType    = "diyapp"
      }

      taints = []

      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"             = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/diyapp-v11-cluster" = "owned"
      }
    }

    monitoring = {
      min_size     = 2
      max_size     = 4
      desired_size = 2

      instance_types = ["t3.large"]
      capacity_type  = "ON_DEMAND"

      labels = {
        Environment = var.environment
        NodeType    = "monitoring"
      }

      taints = [
        {
          key    = "monitoring"
          value  = "true"
          effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
        }
      ]
    }
  }

  node_security_group_additional_rules = {
    ingress_self_all = {
      description = "Node to node all ports/protocols"
      protocol    = "-1"
      from_port   = 0
      to_port     = 0
      type        = "ingress"
      self        = true
    }

    ingress_cluster_ports = {
      description                   = "Cluster API to node group"
      protocol                      = "tcp"
      from_port                     = 1025
      to_port                       = 65535
      type                          = "ingress"
      source_cluster_security_group = true
    }
  }
}

# VPC
module "vpc" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/vpc/aws"
  version = "~> 5.0"

  name = "diyapp-v11-vpc"
  cidr = "10.0.0.0/16"

  azs             = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b", "us-east-1c"]
  private_subnets = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
  public_subnets  = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]

  enable_nat_gateway   = true
  single_nat_gateway   = false
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

# RDS PostgreSQL
module "db" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/rds/aws"
  version = "~> 6.0"

  identifier = "diyapp-v11-db"

  engine               = "postgres"
  engine_version       = "15.3"
  family               = "postgres15"
  major_engine_version = "15"
  instance_class       = "db.t3.medium"

  allocated_storage     = 100
  max_allocated_storage = 500
  storage_encrypted     = true

  db_name  = "diyapp"
  username = var.db_username
  port     = 5432

  multi_az               = true
  db_subnet_group_name   = module.vpc.database_subnet_group_name
  vpc_security_group_ids = [module.vpc.default_security_group_id]

  maintenance_window = "Mon:00:00-Mon:03:00"
  backup_window      = "03:00-06:00"
  backup_retention_period = 7

  performance_insights_enabled          = true
  performance_insights_retention_period = 7
  create_monitoring_role                = true
  monitoring_interval                   = 60

  parameters = [
    {
      name  = "autovacuum"
      value = 1
    },
    {
      name  = "client_encoding"
      value = "utf8"
    }
  ]

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

  snapshot_retention_limit = 7

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core Architecture
# Arquitetura de Microsserviços e Backend-for-Frontend
# Tech Lead: Arquitetura de Sistema V11

"""
ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11
Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceita
Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra + Especialista Backend

CONTEXTO:
A V10 do DIYAPP atingiu limites de escalabilidade devido à arquitetura monolítica.
Necessidade de:
1. Desacoplamento de times para desenvolvimento paralelo (Modo Hive)
2. Escalabilidade independente por domínio de negócio
3. Manutenção de estabilidade 100% autônoma por módulo
4. Suporte a múltiplos frontends (Web, Mobile, Desktop)

DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com padrão Backend-for-Frontend (BFF).
Cada módulo de negócio será um microsserviço independente.
Cada tipo de cliente terá seu próprio BFF que orquestra chamadas aos microsserviços.

OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- Opção A: Monolito modularizado — Prós: Simplicidade inicial, Contras: Acoplamento, dificuldade de escalar
- Opção B: Microsserviços puros — Prós: Desacoplamento máximo, Contras: Complexidade de orquestração no frontend
- Opção C: BFF + Microsserviços — Prós: Desacoplamento + experiência otimizada por cliente, Contras: Duplicação de código BFF
- Opção escolhida: C — Justificativa: Balanceia autonomia dos times com experiência otimizada por plataforma

CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
Positivas: Times podem desenvolver independentemente, deploy independente, escalabilidade granular
Negativas: Complexidade operacional aumentada, necessidade de service discovery, latência de rede
Riscos: Falhas em cascata, versionamento de APIs, consistência de dados eventual
Mitigação: Circuit breakers, API Gateway, contratos de API versionados, eventos assíncronos

REVISÃO: 2024-04-15 (3 meses para avaliação de performance)
"""

# ============================================================================
# ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO V11
# ============================================================================

"""
DIYAPP-V11/
├── README.md
├── docker-compose.yml          # Orquestração local de todos os serviços
├── .github/workflows/          # CI/CD por microsserviço
├── api-gateway/                # API Gateway (Kong/Traefik)
├── bff-web/                    # Backend-for-Frontend Web
├── bff-mobile/                 # BFF Mobile
├── bff-desktop/                # BFF Desktop
├── ms-auth/                    # Microsserviço de Autenticação
├── ms-projects/                # Microsserviço de Projetos
├── ms-templates/               # Microsserviço de Templates
├── ms-execution/               # Microsserviço de Execução de Código
├── ms-monitoring/              # Microsserviço de Monitoramento
├── ms-notifications/           # Microsserviço de Notificações
├── shared/                     # Bibliotecas compartilhadas
│   ├── contracts/              # Contratos de API (OpenAPI/GraphQL)
│   ├── types/                  # Tipos TypeScript compartilhados
│   └── utils/                  # Utilitários comuns
└── infrastructure/             # Terraform/K8s manifests
"""

# ============================================================================
# CONTRATOS DE API - ESPECIFICAÇÃO OPENAPI 3.0
# ============================================================================

# shared/contracts/auth-service.openapi.yaml
auth_service_contract = """
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: Auth Service API
  version: 1.0.0
  description: Microsserviço de autenticação e autorização DIYAPP V11

servers:
  - url: http://ms-auth:3000
    description: Serviço de autenticação

paths:
  /auth/login:
    post:
      summary: Login de usuário
      tags:
        - Auth
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Login bem sucedido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginResponse'
        '401':
          description: Credenciais inválidas

  /auth/validate:
    post:
      summary: Validar token JWT
      tags:
        - Auth
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Token válido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ValidationResponse'

components:
  schemas:
    LoginRequest:
      type: object
      required:
        - email
        - password
      properties:
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
        password:
          type: string
          format: password

    LoginResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        access_token:
          type: string
        refresh_token:
          type: string
        expires_in:
          type: integer
        user:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'

    ValidationResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        valid:
          type: boolean
        user_id:
          type: string
        permissions:
          type: array
          items:
            type: string

  securitySchemes:
    BearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT
"""

# shared/contracts/projects-service.graphql
projects_graphql_schema = """
"""
type Query {
  "Buscar projeto por ID"
  project(id: ID!): Project
  
  "Listar projetos do usuário"
  projects(
    filter: ProjectFilter
    pagination: PaginationInput
  ): ProjectConnection!
  
  "Buscar templates disponíveis"
  templates(category: String): [Template]!
}

type Mutation {
  "Criar novo projeto"
  createProject(input: CreateProjectInput!): Project!
  
  "Atualizar projeto existente"
  updateProject(id: ID!, input: UpdateProjectInput!): Project!
  
  "Executar código do projeto"
  executeProject(id: ID!, input: ExecutionInput!): ExecutionResult!
  
  "Clonar projeto a partir de template"
  cloneFromTemplate(templateId: ID!): Project!
}

type Subscription {
  "Monitorar execução em tempo real"
  executionProgress(projectId: ID!): ExecutionUpdate!
}

type Project {
  id: ID!
  name: String!
  description: String
  code: String!
  language: String!
  dependencies: [Dependency]!
  createdAt: DateTime!
  updatedAt: DateTime!
  lastExecutedAt: DateTime
  executionCount: Int!
  status: ProjectStatus!
  owner: User!
  collaborators: [User]!
}

type ExecutionResult {
  id: ID!
  projectId: ID!
  output: String!
  errors: [ExecutionError]
  executionTime: Float!
  memoryUsage: Float!
  status: ExecutionStatus!
  createdAt: DateTime!
}

input CreateProjectInput {
  name: String!
  description: String
  language: String!
  templateId: ID
  initialCode: String
}

input ExecutionInput {
  parameters: JSON
  timeoutMs: Int = 30000
  memoryLimitMb: Int = 256
}

enum ProjectStatus {
  ACTIVE
  ARCHIVED
  TEMPLATE
}

enum ExecutionStatus {
  PENDING
  RUNNING
  COMPLETED
  FAILED
  TIMEOUT
}

scalar DateTime
scalar JSON
"""

# ============================================================================
# PADRÕES DE COMUNICAÇÃO ENTRE SERVIÇOS
# ============================================================================

"""
ADR-002: Padrões de Comunicação entre Microsserviços
Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceita
Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

CONTEXTO:
Necessidade de definir protocolos de comunicação padronizados entre os
microsserviços para garantir interoperabilidade e resiliência.

DECISÃO:
1. Comunicação síncrona: REST com JSON para operações CRUD simples
2. Comunicação assíncrona: Apache Kafka para eventos de domínio
3. Consultas complexas: GraphQL via BFF para frontends
4. Service Discovery: Consul para descoberta dinâmica de serviços
5. Circuit Breaker: Resilience4j/Polly para tolerância a falhas

OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- Opção A: REST apenas — Prós: Simples, Contras: Over-fetching/under-fetching
- Opção B: GraphQL apenas — Prós: Flexibilidade, Contras: Complexidade, caching
- Opção C: REST + GraphQL + Events — Prós: Ferramenta certa para cada caso, Contras: Maior complexidade
- Opção escolhida: C — Justificativa: Balanceia performance, flexibilidade e resiliência

CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
Positivas: Otimização por caso de uso, resiliência a falhas, evolução independente
Negativas: Maior curva de aprendizado, necessidade de múltiplas bibliotecas
Riscos: Complexidade excessiva, dificuldade de debug distribuído
Mitigação: Documentação clara, tracing distribuído (Jaeger), logs centralizados
"""

# shared/utils/service_client.py
import httpx
import asyncio
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional
from datetime import datetime
import json
import logging
from circuitbreaker import circuit
from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_exponential

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class ServiceClient:
    """Cliente padronizado para comunicação entre microsserviços"""
    
    def __init__(self, service_name: str, base_url: Optional[str] = None):
        self.service_name = service_name
        self.base_url = base_url or self._discover_service(service_name)
        self.client = httpx.AsyncClient(
            timeout=httpx.Timeout(30.0),
            limits=httpx.Limits(max_connections=100, max_keepalive_connections=20),
            transport=httpx.AsyncHTTPTransport(retries=3)
        )
        
    def _discover_service(self, service_name: str) -> str:
        """Descobrir URL do serviço via Consul"""
        # Em produção, consultar Consul API
        # Localmente, usar Docker service names
        service_map = {
            "ms-auth": "http://ms-auth:3000",
            "ms-projects": "http://ms-projects:3001",
            "ms-templates": "http://ms-templates:3002",
            "ms-execution": "http://ms-execution:3003",
            "ms-notifications": "http://ms-notifications:3004"
        }
        return service_map.get(service_name, f"http://{service_name}:3000")
    
    @circuit(failure_threshold=5, expected_exception=httpx.RequestError)
    @retry(
        stop=stop_after_attempt(3),
        wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10)
    )
    async def request(
        self,
        method: str,
        endpoint: str,
        data: Optional[Dict] = None,
        headers: Optional[Dict] = None,
        params: Optional[Dict] = None
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Requisição HTTP padronizada com circuit breaker e retry"""
        url = f"{self.base_url}{endpoint}"
        
        request_headers = {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "User-Agent": f"DIYAPP-ServiceClient/1.0",
            "X-Request-ID": self._generate_request_id(),
            "X-Service-Name": "bff-web",  # Serviço chamador
            **(headers or {})
        }
        
        start_time = datetime.now()
        
        try:
            response = await self.client.request(
                method=method,
                url=url,
                json=data,
                headers=request_headers,
                params=params
            )
            
            duration = (datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds() * 1000
            
            # Log da requisição
            logger.info(
                f"Service call: {method} {url} - "
                f"Status: {response.status_code} - "
                f"Duration: {duration:.2f}ms"
            )
            
            response.raise_for_status()
            
            return response.json()
            
        except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
            logger.error(f"HTTP error from {service_name}: {e.response.status_code}")
            raise
        except httpx.RequestError as e:
            logger.error(f"Request error to {service_name}: {str(e)}")
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Unexpected error calling {service_name}: {str(e)}")
            raise
    
    def _generate_request_id(self) -> str:
        """Gerar ID único para tracing distribuído"""
        import uuid
        return str(uuid.uuid4())
    
    async def close(self):
        """Fechar cliente HTTP"""
        await self.client.aclose()

# BFF (BACKEND-FOR-FRONTEND) - WEB

# bff-web/src/main.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, Depends, HTTPException, WebSocket
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
import graphene
from starlette_graphene3 import GraphQLApp, make_playground_handler
from typing import List
import uvicorn
import logging
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager

from .auth import AuthMiddleware, get_current_user
from .resolvers import Query, Mutation, Subscription
from .services import ProjectService, AuthService, ExecutionService

# Configuração de logging
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("bff-web")

@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    """Gerenciamento de ciclo de vida da aplicação"""
    # Startup
    logger.info("Starting BFF Web service")
    
    # Inicializar clientes de serviço
    app.state.auth_service = AuthService()
    app.state.project_service = ProjectService()
    app.state.execution_service = ExecutionService()
    
    yield
    
    # Shutdown
    logger.info("Shutting down BFF Web service")
    await app.state.auth_service.close()
    await app.state.project_service.close()
    await app.state.execution_service.close()

app = FastAPI(
    title="DIYAPP BFF Web",
    version="1.0.0",
    description="Backend-for-Frontend para interface Web",
    lifespan=lifespan
)

# CORS para desenvolvimento
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["http://localhost:8080", "https://diyapp.example.com"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Middleware de autenticação
app.add_middleware(AuthMiddleware)

# Schema GraphQL
schema = graphene.Schema(
    query=Query,
    mutation=Mutation,
    subscription=Subscription
)

# Endpoint GraphQL
app.add_route(
    "/graphql",
    GraphQLApp(
        schema=schema,
        on_get=make_playground_handler()
    )
)

# Endpoints REST para operações simples
@app.get("/health")
async def health_check():
    """Health check do BFF"""
    services_status = {
        "auth_service": await app.state.auth_service.check_health(),
        "project_service": await app.state.project_service.check_health(),
        "execution_service": await app.state.execution_service.check_health(),
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
    }
    
    all_healthy = all(services_status.values())
    
    return JSONResponse(
        content=services_status,
        status_code=200 if all_healthy else 503
    )

@app.get("/api/projects/summary")
async def get_projects_summary(user = Depends(get_current_user)):
    """Endpoint otimizado para dashboard (BFF pattern)"""
    try:
        # Orquestrar múltiplos microsserviços em uma única chamada
        projects = await app.state.project_service.get_user_projects(user.id)
        recent_executions = await app.state.execution_service.get_recent_executions(user.id)
        templates = await app.state.project_service.get_recommended_templates(user.id)
        
        # Transformar dados para o frontend
        return {
            "projects_count": len(projects),
            "recent_projects": projects[:5],
            "last_executions": recent_executions[:10],
            "suggested_templates": templates,
            "total_execution_time": sum(e.execution_time for e in recent_executions),
            "favorite_languages": self._calculate_favorite_languages(projects)
        }
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error in projects summary: {str(e)}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Internal server error")

@app.websocket("/ws/execution/{project_id}")
async def websocket_execution(websocket: WebSocket, project_id: str):
    """WebSocket para atualizações em tempo real da execução"""
    await websocket.accept()
    
    try:
        # Subscrever no serviço de execução
        async for update in app.state.execution_service.subscribe_to_execution(project_id):
            await websocket.send_json({
                "type": "execution_update",
                "data": update,
                "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
            })
            
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"WebSocket error: {str(e)}")
        await websocket.close(code=1011)

    """Serviço de orquestração para projetos"""

# src/core/config.py
import os
from typing import Optional
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from pydantic import Field, RedisDsn, PostgresDsn, validator


class Settings(BaseSettings):
    """Configurações da aplicação com validação de tipos"""
    
    # API
    APP_NAME: str = "DIYAPP V11 Core"
    APP_VERSION: str = "v1.0.0"
    API_V1_PREFIX: str = "/api/v1"
    DEBUG: bool = Field(default=False, env="DEBUG")
    
    # Redis
    REDIS_URL: RedisDsn = Field(
        default="redis://localhost:6379/0",
        env="REDIS_URL"
    )
    REDIS_CACHE_TTL: int = Field(default=300, env="REDIS_CACHE_TTL")  # 5 minutos
    REDIS_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TTL: int = Field(default=60, env="REDIS_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TTL")  # 1 minuto
    
    # PostgreSQL
    DATABASE_URL: PostgresDsn = Field(
        default="postgresql://user:pass@localhost:5432/diyapp",
        env="DATABASE_URL"
    )
    
    # Celery (RabbitMQ/Redis)
    CELERY_BROKER_URL: str = Field(
        default="redis://localhost:6379/1",
        env="CELERY_BROKER_URL"
    )
    CELERY_RESULT_BACKEND: str = Field(
        default="redis://localhost:6379/2",
        env="CELERY_RESULT_BACKEND"
    )
    
    # Circuit Breaker
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD: int = Field(default=5, env="CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD")
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT: int = Field(default=30, env="CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT")
    
    # Rate Limiting
    RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: int = Field(default=100, env="RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS")
    RATE_LIMIT_PERIOD: int = Field(default=60, env="RATE_LIMIT_PERIOD")  # segundos
    
    # Timeouts
    EXTERNAL_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = Field(default=10, env="EXTERNAL_SERVICE_TIMEOUT")  # segundos
    DATABASE_TIMEOUT: int = Field(default=5, env="DATABASE_TIMEOUT")
    CACHE_TIMEOUT: int = Field(default=2, env="CACHE_TIMEOUT")
    
    # Observability
    LOG_LEVEL: str = Field(default="INFO", env="LOG_LEVEL")
    METRICS_PORT: int = Field(default=9090, env="METRICS_PORT")
    ENABLE_TRACING: bool = Field(default=False, env="ENABLE_TRACING")
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = True
    
    @validator("REDIS_URL", "DATABASE_URL", "CELERY_BROKER_URL", pre=True)
    def validate_urls(cls, v):
        if isinstance(v, str) and v == "":
            raise ValueError("URL não pode ser vazia")
        return v


settings = Settings()

# src/core/exceptions.py
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional
from fastapi import HTTPException, status


class DIYAppException(Exception):
    """Base exception para a aplicação"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str,
        status_code: int = status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
        detail: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
        internal_code: Optional[str] = None
    ):
        self.message = message
        self.status_code = status_code
        self.detail = detail or {}
        self.internal_code = internal_code
        super().__init__(message)


class ServiceUnavailableException(DIYAppException):
    """Serviço externo indisponível"""
    
    def __init__(self, service_name: str, detail: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(
            message=f"Serviço {service_name} temporariamente indisponível",
            status_code=status.HTTP_503_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,
            detail=detail or {"service": service_name},
            internal_code="SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE"
        )


class CircuitBreakerOpenException(DIYAppException):
    """Circuit breaker aberto para um serviço"""
    
    def __init__(self, service_name: str, retry_after: int = 30):
        super().__init__(
            message=f"Serviço {service_name} em modo de recuperação",
            status_code=status.HTTP_503_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,
            detail={
                "service": service_name,
                "retry_after": retry_after,
                "code": "CIRCUIT_BREAKER_OPEN"
            },
            internal_code="CIRCUIT_BREAKER_OPEN"
        )


class CacheException(DIYAppException):
    """Exceção relacionada ao cache"""
    
    def __init__(self, operation: str, key: str, detail: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(
            message=f"Falha na operação de cache: {operation} para chave {key}",
            status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
            detail=detail or {"operation": operation, "key": key},
            internal_code="CACHE_ERROR"
        )


class QueueException(DIYAppException):
    """Exceção relacionada a filas"""
    
    def __init__(self, queue_name: str, task_id: Optional[str] = None):
        super().__init__(
            message=f"Falha na fila {queue_name}",
            status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
            detail={"queue": queue_name, "task_id": task_id},
            internal_code="QUEUE_ERROR"
        )


class RateLimitException(DIYAppException):
    """Rate limit excedido"""
    
    def __init__(self, limit: int, window: int):
        super().__init__(
            message="Limite de requisições excedido",
            status_code=status.HTTP_429_TOO_MANY_REQUESTS,
            detail={
                "limit": limit,
                "window": window,
                "retry_after": window,
                "code": "RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED"
            },
            internal_code="RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED"
        )

# src/utils/logger.py
import structlog
import logging
import sys
from typing import Any, Dict
from datetime import datetime
from uuid import uuid4


def setup_logging(level: str = "INFO") -> structlog.BoundLogger:
    """Configura logging estruturado com correlation ID"""
    
    # Remove handlers existentes
    for handler in logging.root.handlers[:]:
        logging.root.removeHandler(handler)
    
    # Configura structlog
    structlog.configure(
        processors=[
            structlog.contextvars.merge_contextvars,
            structlog.processors.add_log_level,
            structlog.processors.StackInfoRenderer(),
            structlog.dev.set_exc_info,
            structlog.processors.TimeStamper(fmt="iso"),
            structlog.processors.JSONRenderer()
        ],
        wrapper_class=structlog.BoundLogger,
        logger_factory=structlog.PrintLoggerFactory(),
        cache_logger_on_first_use=True,
    )
    
    # Configura logging padrão
    logging.basicConfig(
        format="%(message)s",
        stream=sys.stdout,
        level=getattr(logging, level.upper())
    )
    
    return structlog.get_logger()


class RequestContext:
    """Context manager para request com correlation ID"""
    
    def __init__(self, correlation_id: str = None, user_id: str = None):
        self.correlation_id = correlation_id or str(uuid4())
        self.user_id = user_id
        self._contextvars = structlog.contextvars
        
    def __enter__(self):
        self._contextvars.bind_contextvars(
            correlation_id=self.correlation_id,
            user_id=self.user_id,
            timestamp=datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
        )
        return self
    
    def __exit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):
        self._contextvars.clear_contextvars()


# src/utils/metrics.py
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge, generate_latest
from typing import Optional, Callable
import time


class MetricsCollector:
    """Coletor de métricas para observabilidade"""
    
    # HTTP Metrics
    http_requests_total = Counter(
        'http_requests_total',
        'Total HTTP requests',
        ['method', 'endpoint', 'status']
    )
    
    http_request_duration_seconds = Histogram(
        'http_request_duration_seconds',
        'HTTP request duration in seconds',
        ['method', 'endpoint'],
        buckets=[0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.3, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0]
    )
    
    # Cache Metrics
    cache_hits_total = Counter(
        'cache_hits_total',
        'Total cache hits',
        ['cache_name', 'operation']
    )
    
    cache_misses_total = Counter(
        'cache_misses_total',
        'Total cache misses',
        ['cache_name', 'operation']
    )
    
    cache_operations_duration_seconds = Histogram(
        'cache_operations_duration_seconds',
        'Cache operations duration',
        ['cache_name', 'operation'],
        buckets=[0.001, 0.005, 0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.5]
    )
    
    # Circuit Breaker Metrics
    circuit_breaker_state = Gauge(
        'circuit_breaker_state',
        'Circuit breaker state (0=closed, 1=open, 2=half-open)',
        ['service_name']
    )
    
    circuit_breaker_failures_total = Counter(
        'circuit_breaker_failures_total',
        'Total circuit breaker failures',
        ['service_name']
    )
    
    # Queue Metrics
    queue_tasks_total = Counter(
        'queue_tasks_total',
        'Total queue tasks',
        ['queue_name', 'task_type', 'status']
    )
    
    queue_task_duration_seconds = Histogram(
        'queue_task_duration_seconds',
        'Queue task duration in seconds',
        ['queue_name', 'task_type'],
        buckets=[0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 5.0, 10.0, 30.0, 60.0]
    )
    
    @classmethod
    def track_request(cls, method: str, endpoint: str, status: int):
        """Track HTTP request"""
        cls.http_requests_total.labels(
            method=method,
            endpoint=endpoint,
            status=status
        ).inc()
    
    @classmethod
    def track_request_duration(cls, method: str, endpoint: str, duration: float):
        """Track HTTP request duration"""
        cls.http_request_duration_seconds.labels(
            method=method,
            endpoint=endpoint
        ).observe(duration)
    
    @classmethod
    def track_cache_operation(
        cls,
        cache_name: str,
        operation: str,
        hit: bool,
        duration: float
    ):
        """Track cache operation"""
        if hit:
            cls.cache_hits_total.labels(
                cache_name=cache_name,
                operation=operation
            ).inc()
        else:
            cls.cache_misses_total.labels(
                cache_name=cache_name,
                operation=operation
            ).inc()
        
        cls.cache_operations_duration_seconds.labels(
            cache_name=cache_name,
            operation=operation
        ).observe(duration)
    
    @classmethod
    def track_circuit_breaker_state(cls, service_name: str, state: int):
        """Track circuit breaker state"""
        cls.circuit_breaker_state.labels(
            service_name=service_name
        ).set(state)
    
    @classmethod
    def track_circuit_breaker_failure(cls, service_name: str):
        """Track circuit breaker failure"""
        cls.circuit_breaker_failures_total.labels(
            service_name=service_name
        ).inc()
    
    @classmethod
    def track_queue_task(
        cls,
        queue_name: str,
        task_type: str,
        status: str,
        duration: Optional[float] = None
    ):
        """Track queue task"""
        cls.queue_tasks_total.labels(
            queue_name=queue_name,
            task_type=task_type,
            status=status
        ).inc()
        
        if duration is not None:
            cls.queue_task_duration_seconds.labels(
                queue_name=queue_name,
                task_type=task_type
            ).observe(duration)
    
    @classmethod
    def get_metrics(cls):
        """Retorna métricas no formato Prometheus"""
        return generate_latest()


# src/services/circuit_breaker.py
import time
from typing import Optional, Callable, Any
from enum import Enum
from dataclasses import dataclass
from src.core.config import settings
from src.utils.metrics import MetricsCollector
from src.core.exceptions import CircuitBreakerOpenException
import redis
from functools import wraps


class CircuitState(Enum):
    CLOSED = "CLOSED"
    OPEN = "OPEN"
    HALF_OPEN = "HALF_OPEN"


@dataclass
class CircuitBreakerStats:
    failures: int = 0
    successes: int = 0
    last_failure_time: Optional[float] = None
    state: CircuitState = CircuitState.CLOSED


class CircuitBreaker:
    """Implementação de Circuit Breaker com Redis para estado distribuído"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        service_name: str,
        failure_threshold: Optional[int] = None,
        recovery_timeout: Optional[int] = None,
        redis_client: Optional[redis.Redis] = None
    ):
        self.service_name = service_name
        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold or settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD
        self.recovery_timeout = recovery_timeout or settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT
        self.redis_client = redis_client
        self._local_stats = CircuitBreakerStats()
        
    def _get_redis_key(self, key_suffix: str) -> str:
        """Gera chave Redis para o circuit breaker"""
        return f"circuit_breaker:{self.service_name}:{key_suffix}"
    
    def _get_stats_from_redis(self) -> Optional[CircuitBreakerStats]:
        """Recupera estatísticas do Redis"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return None
            
        try:
            data = self.redis_client.get(self._get_redis_key("stats"))
            if data:
                import json
                stats_dict = json.loads(data)
                return CircuitBreakerStats(
                   

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core: Observabilidade de IA e Retreinamento Automático

Vou criar um sistema completo de observabilidade de IA com MLflow e Weights & Biases, integrado com pipelines de retreinamento automático baseado em drift de dados.

```python
# Estrutura do projeto
# ├── src/
# │   ├── __init__.py
# │   ├── ai_observability/
# │   │   ├── __init__.py
# │   │   ├── mlflow_tracker.py
# │   │   ├── wandb_tracker.py
# │   │   ├── drift_detector.py
# │   │   └── retraining_pipeline.py
# │   ├── models/
# │   │   ├── __init__.py
# │   │   └── llm_monitor.py
# │   ├── api/
# │   │   ├── __init__.py
# │   │   └── endpoints.py
# │   └── utils/
# │       ├── __init__.py
# │       └── config.py
# ├── public/
# │   ├── index.html
# │   ├── css/

# │   └── js/

## 2. config/settings.yaml

```yaml
observability:
  mlflow:
    tracking_uri: "http://localhost:5000"
    experiment_name: "llm_production"
    registry_uri: "sqlite:///mlflow.db"
  
  wandb:
    project: "diyapp-llm-observability"
    entity: "diyapp-team"
    api_key: "${WANDB_API_KEY}"
  
  drift_detection:
    threshold: 0.10  # 10% drift threshold
    window_size: 1000
    check_interval_hours: 24
    
  retraining:
    enabled: true
    min_samples: 10000
    trigger_threshold: 0.15
    schedule: "0 2 * * *"  # Daily at 2 AM
  
  providers:
    anthropic:
      cost_per_token_input: 0.000015
      cost_per_token_output: 0.000075
    openai:
      cost_per_token_input: 0.00001
      cost_per_token_output: 0.00003
    google:
      cost_per_token_input: 0.000007
      cost_per_token_output: 0.000021
  
  metrics:
    latency_slo_ms: 8000
    availability_slo: 0.99
    error_rate_slo: 0.01
    fallback_rate_slo: 0.05

database:
  postgres:
    host: "localhost"
    port: 5432
    database: "ai_observability"
    user: "${DB_USER}"
    password: "${DB_PASSWORD}"
  
  redis:
    host: "localhost"
    port: 6379

logging:
  level: "INFO"
  file: "logs/ai_ops.log"
  format: "%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"
```

## 3. src/utils/config.py

```python
import os
import yaml
from typing import Dict, Any
from pydantic import BaseSettings, Field
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    """Configurações da aplicação"""
    
    # MLflow
    mlflow_tracking_uri: str = Field(default="http://localhost:5000")
    mlflow_experiment_name: str = Field(default="llm_production")
    
    # Weights & Biases
    wandb_project: str = Field(default="diyapp-llm-observability")
    wandb_entity: str = Field(default="diyapp-team")
    wandb_api_key: str = Field(default="")
    
    # Database
    db_host: str = Field(default="localhost")
    db_port: int = Field(default=5432)
    db_name: str = Field(default="ai_observability")
    db_user: str = Field(default="postgres")
    db_password: str = Field(default="")
    
    # Redis
    redis_host: str = Field(default="localhost")
    redis_port: int = Field(default=6379)
    
    # Drift Detection
    drift_threshold: float = Field(default=0.10)
    drift_window_size: int = Field(default=1000)
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"

class ConfigLoader:
    """Carregador de configurações YAML"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def load_config(config_path: str = "config/settings.yaml") -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Carrega configurações do arquivo YAML"""
        with open(config_path, 'r') as f:
            config = yaml.safe_load(f)
        
        # Substitui variáveis de ambiente
        config_str = yaml.dump(config)
        config_str = os.path.expandvars(config_str)
        config = yaml.safe_load(config_str)
        
        return config
    
    @staticmethod
    def get_provider_costs() -> Dict[str, Dict[str, float]]:
        """Retorna custos por provedor"""
        config = ConfigLoader.load_config()
        return config['observability']['providers']

settings = Settings()
config = ConfigLoader.load_config()
```

## 4. src/ai_observability/mlflow_tracker.py

```python
import mlflow
import mlflow.sklearn
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
import pandas as pd
import json
from ..utils.config import settings

class MLflowTracker:
    """Tracker de experimentos usando MLflow"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        mlflow.set_tracking_uri(settings.mlflow_tracking_uri)
        mlflow.set_experiment(settings.mlflow_experiment_name)
        
    def log_llm_call(
        self,
        model_name: str,
        provider: str,
        feature: str,
        input_tokens: int,
        output_tokens: int,
        latency_ms: float,
        cost: float,
        success: bool = True,
        error_message: Optional[str] = None,
        metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    ):
        """Log de uma chamada LLM"""
        
        with mlflow.start_run(run_name=f"llm_call_{datetime.now().isoformat()}", nested=True):
            # Log de métricas básicas
            mlflow.log_metric("input_tokens", input_tokens)
            mlflow.log_metric("output_tokens", output_tokens)
            mlflow.log_metric("total_tokens", input_tokens + output_tokens)
            mlflow.log_metric("latency_ms", latency_ms)
            mlflow.log_metric("cost", cost)
            mlflow.log_metric("success", 1 if success else 0)
            
            # Log de parâmetros
            mlflow.log_param("model_name", model_name)
            mlflow.log_param("provider", provider)
            mlflow.log_param("feature", feature)
            
            # Log de tags
            mlflow.set_tag("call_type", "llm_inference")
            mlflow.set_tag("timestamp", datetime.now().isoformat())
            
            if error_message:
                mlflow.log_param("error_message", error_message)
                mlflow.set_tag("status", "error")
            else:
                mlflow.set_tag("status", "success")
            
            # Log de metadados adicionais
            if metadata:
                mlflow.log_dict(metadata, "metadata.json")
    
    def log_model_performance(
        self,
        model_name: str,
        metrics: Dict[str, float],
        dataset_name: str,
        timestamp: datetime = None
    ):
        """Log de performance do modelo no golden dataset"""
        
        if timestamp is None:
            timestamp = datetime.now()
            
        with mlflow.start_run(run_name=f"eval_{model_name}_{timestamp.strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"):
            # Log de todas as métricas
            for metric_name, value in metrics.items():
                mlflow.log_metric(metric_name, value)
            
            # Log de parâmetros
            mlflow.log_param("model_name", model_name)
            mlflow.log_param("dataset_name", dataset_name)
            mlflow.log_param("evaluation_timestamp", timestamp.isoformat())
            
            mlflow.set_tag("evaluation_type", "golden_dataset")
            mlflow.set_tag("model_version", model_name)
    
    def log_drift_detection(
        self,
        feature: str,
        drift_score: float,
        drift_type: str,
        threshold: float,
        is_drift: bool,
        sample_size: int,
        detection_time: datetime = None
    ):
        """Log de detecção de drift"""
        
        if detection_time is None:
            detection_time = datetime.now()
            
        with mlflow.start_run(run_name=f"drift_{feature}_{detection_time.strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"):
            mlflow.log_metric("drift_score", drift_score)
            mlflow.log_metric("threshold", threshold)
            mlflow.log_metric("sample_size", sample_size)
            mlflow.log_metric("is_drift", 1 if is_drift else 0)
            
            mlflow.log_param("feature", feature)
            mlflow.log_param("drift_type", drift_type)
            mlflow.log_param("detection_time", detection_time.isoformat())
            
            mlflow.set_tag("detection_type", "drift")
            mlflow.set_tag("status", "drift_detected" if is_drift else "no_drift")
    
    def get_model_performance_history(
        self,
        model_name: str,
        days: int = 30
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """Recupera histórico de performance do modelo"""
        
        from datetime import datetime, timedelta
        
        end_time = datetime.now()
        start_time = end_time - timedelta(days=days)
        
        # Converte para timestamp em milissegundos
        start_time_ms = int(start_time.timestamp() * 1000)
        end_time_ms = int(end_time.timestamp() * 1000)
        
        # Busca runs do MLflow
        experiment = mlflow.get_experiment_by_name(settings.mlflow_experiment_name)
        if experiment is None:
            return pd.DataFrame()
        
        runs = mlflow.search_runs(
            experiment_ids=[experiment.experiment_id],
            filter_string=f"params.model_name = '{model_name}' AND tags.evaluation_type = 'golden_dataset'",
            start_time=start_time_ms,
            end_time=end_time_ms
        )
        
        return runs
    
    def register_model(
        self,
        model,
        model_name: str,
        metrics: Dict[str, float],
        description: str = ""
    ):
        """Registra um novo modelo no MLflow Model Registry"""
        
        with mlflow.start_run(run_name=f"register_{model_name}_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"):
            # Log do modelo
            mlflow.sklearn.log_model(model, "model")
            
            # Log das métricas
            for metric_name, value in metrics.items():
                mlflow.log_metric(metric_name, value)
            
            # Registra o modelo
            model_uri = f"runs:/{mlflow.active_run().info.run_id}/model"
            registered_model = mlflow.register_model(model_uri, model_name)
            
            # Adiciona descrição
            mlflow.update_registered_model(
                name=model_name,
                description=description
            )
            
            return registered_model
```

## 5. src/ai_observability/wandb_tracker.py

```python
import wandb
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
import pandas as pd
import plotly.graph_objects as go
from plotly.subplots import make_subplots
from ..utils.config import settings

class WandBTracker:
    """Tracker de experimentos usando Weights & Biases"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.run = None
        self.initialized = False
        
    def init_run(self, run_name: Optional[str] = None):
        """Inicializa uma nova run no W&B"""
        if not settings.wandb_api_key:
            print("WARNING: W&B API key not set. Skipping W&B initialization.")
            return
            
        if run_name is None:
            run_name = f"llm_observability_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
        
        self.run = wandb.init(
            project=settings.wandb_project,
            entity=settings.wandb_entity,
            name=run_name,
            config={
                "drift_threshold": settings.drift_threshold,
                "window_size": settings.drift_window_size
            }
        )
        self.initialized = True
    
    def log_llm_metrics_batch(
        self,
        metrics_df: pd.DataFrame,
        step: Optional[int] = None
    ):
        """Log de métricas de LLM em batch"""
        if not self.initialized or self.run is None:
            return
        
        # Calcula métricas agregadas
        summary_metrics = {
            "total_calls": len(metrics_df),
            "avg_latency_ms": metrics_df['latency_ms'].mean(),
            "avg_input_tokens": metrics_df['input_tokens'].mean(),
            "avg_output_tokens": metrics_df['output_tokens'].mean(),
            "total_cost": metrics_df['cost'].sum(),
            "success_rate": metrics_df['success'].mean() if 'success' in metrics_df.columns else 1.0
        }
        
        # Log das métricas
        self.run.log(summary_metrics, step=step)
        
        # Log de histogramas
        if len(metrics_df) > 0:
            self.run.log({
                "latency_distribution": wandb.Histogram(metrics_df['latency_ms'].values),
                "input_tokens_distribution": wandb.Histogram(metrics_df['input_tokens'].values),
                "output_tokens_distribution": wandb.Histogram(metrics_df['output_tokens'].values),
                "cost_distribution": wandb.Histogram(metrics_df['cost'].values)
            }, step=step)
    
    def log_drift_analysis(
        self,
        feature: str,
        reference_data: pd.DataFrame,
        current_data: pd.DataFrame,
        drift_metrics: Dict[str, float],
        plots: Dict[str, go.Figure]
    ):
        """Log de análise de drift"""
        if not self.initialized or self.run is None:
            return
        
        # Log das métricas de drift
        self.run.log({
            f"drift/{feature}/ks_statistic": drift_metrics.get('ks_statistic', 0),
            f"drift/{feature}/psi": drift_metrics.get('psi', 0),
            f"drift/{feature}/mmd": drift_metrics.get('mmd', 0),
            f"drift/{feature}/is_drift": drift_metrics.get('is_drift', False)
        })
        
        # Log dos plots
        for plot_name, plot in plots.items():
            self.run.log({f"drift_plots/{feature}/{plot_name}": wandb.Plotly(plot)})
        
        # Log de tabelas de dados
        self.run.log({
            f"drift_data/{feature}/reference_stats": wandb.Table(dataframe=reference_data.describe()),
            f"drift_data/{feature}/current_stats": wandb.Table(dataframe=current_data.describe())
        })
    
    def create_cost_dashboard(
        self,
        cost_data: pd.DataFrame,
        time_column: str = "timestamp"
    ) -> go.Figure:
        """Cria dashboard de custos"""
        
        fig = make_subplots(
            rows=2, cols=2,
            subplot_titles=("Custo Total por Dia", "Custo por Provedor", 
                          "Custo por Feature", "Tokens por Chamada"),
            specs=[[{"type": "scatter"}, {"type": "pie"}],
                   [{"type": "bar"}, {"type": "box"}]]
        )
        
        # 1. Custo total por dia
        daily_cost = cost_data.groupby(pd.Grouper(key=time_column, freq='D'))['cost'].sum().reset_index()
        fig.add_trace(
            go.Scatter(x=daily_cost[time_column], y=daily_cost['cost'], 
                      mode='lines+markers', name='Custo Diário'),
            row=1, col=1
        )
        
        # 2. Custo por provedor
        provider_cost = cost_data.groupby('provider')['cost'].sum().reset_index()
        fig.add_trace(
            go.Pie(labels=provider_cost['provider'], values=provider_cost['cost'],
                   name='Custo por Provedor'),
            row=1, col=2
        )
        
        # 3. Custo por feature
        feature_cost = cost_data.groupby('feature')['cost'].sum().sort_values(ascending=False).head(10)
        fig.add_trace(
            go.Bar(x=

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Design System e Wireframes

Vou criar um Design System completo para a V11 com tokens de design, componentes e guidelines, seguido de wireframes de alta fidelidade para todas as views principais.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-design-system/
├── index.html (Dashboard/Interface Principal)
├── design-system/
│   ├── tokens.css
│   ├── components.css
│   └── guidelines.html
├── wireframes/
│   ├── dashboard.html
│   ├── project-builder.html
│   ├── ai-assistant.html
│   ├── analytics.html
│   └── settings.html
├── prototypes/
│   └── interactive-prototype.js
├── assets/
│   ├── icons/
│   └── fonts/
└── README.md
```

## 1. Design System - Tokens e Componentes

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. ADRs (Architecture Decision Records)

### `docs/architecture/ADR-001-service-boundaries.md`

```markdown
# ADR-001: Definição de Boundaries de Microsserviços

## Status
Aceito

## Data
2024-01-15

## Contexto
Precisamos decompor a aplicação monolítica DIYAPP em microsserviços para:
- Escalabilidade independente
- Isolamento de falhas
- Time de desenvolvimento paralelo
- Deploy independente

## Decisão
Dividir a aplicação em 4 serviços core:

1. **Auth Service** (Porta: 3001)
   - Autenticação JWT
   - Autorização RBAC
   - Gerenciamento de sessões
   - OAuth2 providers

2. **User Service** (Porta: 3002)
   - Perfis de usuário
   - Preferências
   - Upload de avatar
   - Configurações

3. **Task Service** (Porta: 3003)
   - CRUD de tarefas
   - Categorias e tags
   - Busca e filtros
   - Estatísticas

4. **Notification Service** (Porta: 3004)
   - Email (SMTP)
   - WhatsApp (Baileys)
   - WebSocket para notificações em tempo real
   - Template engine

5. **API Gateway** (Porta: 3000)
   - Roteamento
   - Rate limiting
   - Circuit breaker
   - Logging centralizado

## Opções Consideradas

### Opção A: 6 serviços (separar File Service)
- Prós: Escalabilidade específica para uploads
- Contras: Complexidade adicional, mais comunicação síncrona

### Opção B: 3 serviços (combinar Auth + User)
- Prós: Menos serviços para gerenciar
- Contras: Acoplamento alto, dificulta escalabilidade

### Opção Escolhida: 4 serviços + Gateway
- Justificativa: Balanceamento entre granularidade e complexidade operacional

## Consequências
### Positivas
- Escalabilidade independente por domínio
- Falhas isoladas por serviço
- Times podem trabalhar em paralelo

### Negativas
- Complexidade de deploy aumentada
- Necessidade de orquestração (Docker Compose/K8s)
- Comunicação entre serviços requer padrões

### Riscos
- Latência em chamadas entre serviços
- Consistência eventual em alguns cenários
- Monitoramento distribuído necessário

## Revisão
2024-04-15 (reavaliar após 3 meses em produção)
```

### `docs/architecture/ADR-002-api-gateway.md`

```markdown
# ADR-002: Implementação de API Gateway com Express + Node.js

## Status
Aceito

## Data
2024-01-15

## Contexto
Necessidade de ponto único de entrada para:
- Roteamento de requisições
- Autenticação centralizada
- Rate limiting
- Logging unificado
- Transformação de respostas

## Decisão
Implementar API Gateway customizado com:
- Express.js como framework
- http-proxy-middleware para roteamento
- Redis para rate limiting e cache
- Winston para logging estruturado
- Circuit breaker com opossum

## Configuração de Roteamento:
```yaml
/auth/*    → auth-service:3001
/users/*   → user-service:3002
/tasks/*   → task-service:3003
/notify/*  → notification-service:3004
```

## Opções Consideradas
### Opção A: Kong/API Gateway dedicado
- Prós: Feature-rich, enterprise-ready
- Contras: Overhead, curva de aprendizado

### Opção B: Nginx como reverse proxy
- Prós: Performance, simplicidade
- Contras: Lógica de negócio limitada

### Opção Escolhida: Express customizado
- Justificativa: Controle total, stack consistente, fácil debug

## Consequências
### Positivas
- Controle completo sobre lógica de roteamento
- Stack consistente com serviços
- Fácil extensão com middleware

### Negativas
- Manutenção própria
- Performance inferior a Nginx puro

## Revisão
2024-03-15
```

## 2. Contratos de API (OpenAPI 3.0)

### `docs/api/openapi/auth-service.yaml`

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.0
info:
  title: Auth Service API
  version: 1.0.0
  description: Serviço de autenticação e autorização DIYAPP

servers:
  - url: http://localhost:3001
    description: Local development
  - url: https://auth.diyapp.com
    description: Production

tags:
  - name: Authentication
    description: Operações de login/logout
  - name: Authorization
    description: Controle de acesso

paths:
  /auth/login:
    post:
      tags: [Authentication]
      summary: Login de usuário
      operationId: loginUser
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Login bem-sucedido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginResponse'
        '401':
          description: Credenciais inválidas
        '429':
          description: Too many requests

  /auth/register:
    post:
      tags: [Authentication]
      summary: Registro de novo usuário
      operationId: registerUser
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/RegisterRequest'
      responses:
        '201':
          description: Usuário criado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/UserResponse'
        '400':
          description: Dados inválidos
        '409':
          description: Usuário já existe

  /auth/verify/{token}:
    get:
      tags: [Authentication]
      summary: Verificar token JWT
      operationId: verifyToken
      parameters:
        - name: token
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Token válido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  valid:
                    type: boolean
                  user:
                    $ref: '#/components/schemas/UserInfo'
        '401':
          description: Token inválido ou expirado

components:
  schemas:
    LoginRequest:
      type: object
      required: [email, password]
      properties:
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
          example: user@example.com
        password:
          type: string
          format: password
          minLength: 8
          example: "SecurePass123!"

    LoginResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        accessToken:
          type: string
          description: JWT token para autenticação
        refreshToken:
          type: string
          description: Token para renovar acesso
        expiresIn:
          type: integer
          description: Segundos até expiração
        user:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/UserInfo'

    RegisterRequest:
      type: object
      required: [email, password, name]
      properties:
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
        password:
          type: string
          format: password
          minLength: 8
        name:
          type: string
          minLength: 2
        phone:
          type: string
          pattern: '^\+?[1-9]\d{1,14}$'

    UserInfo:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        email:
          type: string
        name:
          type: string
        role:
          type: string
          enum: [user, admin, moderator]

securitySchemes:
  BearerAuth:
    type: http
    scheme: bearer
    bearerFormat: JWT
```

## 3. Código Base - API Gateway

### `src/api-gateway/Dockerfile`

```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Instalar dependências
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copiar código
COPY . .

# Configurar usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs
RUN adduser -S nodejs -u 1001
USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node healthcheck.js

EXPOSE 3000

CMD ["node", "src/index.js"]
```

### `src/api-gateway/package.json`

```json
{
  "name": "@diyapp/api-gateway",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "API Gateway for DIYAPP V11",
  "main": "src/index.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node src/index.js",
    "dev": "nodemon src/index.js",
    "test": "jest",
    "test:watch": "jest --watch",
    "lint": "eslint src/",
    "lint:fix": "eslint src/ --fix",
    "format": "prettier --write src/",
    "docker:build": "docker build -t diyapp/api-gateway .",
    "docker:run": "docker run -p 3000:3000 diyapp/api-gateway"

    "jest": "^29.5.0",

  },
  "engines": {
    "node": ">=18.0.0"
  }
}
```

### `src/api-gateway/src/index.js`

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const { createProxyMiddleware } = require('http-proxy-middleware');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const compression = require('compression');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const logger = require('./shared/lib/logger');
const errorHandler = require('./middleware/error-handler');
const authMiddleware = require('./middleware/auth');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Configuração de segurança
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
    },
  },
}));

// CORS configurável
const corsOptions = {
  origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN?.split(',') || ['http://localhost:8080'],
  credentials: true,
  optionsSuccessStatus: 200,
};
app.use(cors(corsOptions));

// Compressão
app.use(compression());

// Rate limiting global
const globalLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
  max: 100, // limite por IP
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP',
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
});
app.use(globalLimiter);

// Logging middleware
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  logger.info(`${req.method} ${req.url}`, {
    ip: req.ip,
    userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
  });
  next();
});

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    service: 'api-gateway',
    version: process.env.npm_package_version || '1.0.0',
  });
});

// Configuração de proxies para serviços
const services = {
  auth: {
    target: process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_URL || 'http://auth-service:3001',
    pathRewrite: { '^/auth': '' },
    changeOrigin: true,
    onProxyReq: (proxyReq, req) => {
      logger.debug(`Proxying to auth service: ${req.method} ${req.url}`);
    },
  },
  users: {
    target: process.env.USER_SERVICE_URL || 'http://user-service:3002',
    pathRewrite: { '^/users': '' },
    changeOrigin: true,
  },
  tasks: {
    target: process.env.TASK_SERVICE_URL || 'http://task-service:3003',
    pathRewrite: { '^/tasks': '' },
    changeOrigin: true,
  },
  notify: {
    target: process.env.NOTIFY_SERVICE_URL || 'http://notification-service:3004',
    pathRewrite: { '^/notify': '' },
    changeOrigin: true,
  },
};

// Aplicar middleware de autenticação para rotas protegidas
app.use('/auth/*', createProxyMiddleware(services.auth));
app.use('/users/*', authMiddleware.verifyToken, createProxyMiddleware(services.users));
app.use('/tasks/*', authMiddleware.verifyToken, createProxyMiddleware(services.tasks));
app.use('/notify/*', authMiddleware.verifyToken, createProxyMiddleware(services.notify));

// Rota para documentação OpenAPI
app.use('/api-docs', express.static('docs/api/openapi'));

// 404 handler
app.use((req, res) => {
  logger.warn(`Route not found: ${req.method} ${req.url}`);
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Not Found',
    message: `Cannot ${req.method} ${req.url}`,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  });
});

// Error handler global
app.use(errorHandler);

// Iniciar servidor
const server = app.listen(PORT, () => {
  logger.info(`API Gateway running on port ${PORT}`);
  logger.info(`Environment: ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'}`);
});

// Graceful shutdown
const shutdown = () => {
  logger.info('Received shutdown signal');
  server.close(() => {
    logger.info('Server closed');
    process.exit(0);
  });

  setTimeout(() => {
    logger.error('Forced shutdown after timeout');
    process.exit(1);
  }, 10000);
};

process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown);
process.on('SIGINT', shutdown);

module.exports = app;
```

### `src/api-gateway/src/middleware/auth.js`

```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const logger = require('../shared/lib/logger');
const { UnauthorizedError, ForbiddenError } =

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes de alta-fidelidade e fluxos de onboarding, focando em dark/light mode e acessibilidade WCAG AA.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-design-system/
├── index.html
├── style.css
├── design-tokens.js
├── components/
│   ├── button.js
│   ├── card.js
│   ├── modal.js
│   ├── navigation.js
│   ├── metrics.js
│   └── onboarding.js
├── pages/
│   ├── dashboard.html
│   ├── onboarding.html
│   └── metrics.html
└── assets/
    ├── icons/
    └── illustrations/
```

## 1. Design Tokens (design-tokens.js)

```javascript
// design-tokens.js
class DesignTokens {
  constructor() {
    this.tokens = {
      version: "v1.0.0",
      lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString(),
      
      // Color Palette - WCAG AA Compliant

  // Get CSS custom properties for light mode
  getLightModeCSS() {
    return `
      :root {
        /* Color Tokens */
        --color-primary-50: ${this.tokens.colors.primary[50]};
        --color-primary-500: ${this.tokens.colors.primary[500]};
        --color-primary-700: ${this.tokens.colors.primary[700]};
        
        --color-neutral-0: ${this.tokens.colors.neutral[0]};
        --color-neutral-100: ${this.tokens.colors.neutral[100]};
        --color-neutral-200: ${this.tokens.colors.neutral[200]};
        --color-neutral-500: ${this.tokens.colors.neutral[500]};
        --color-neutral-700: ${this.tokens.colors.neutral[700]};
        --color-neutral-900: ${this.tokens.colors.neutral[900]};
        
        --color-success: ${this.tokens.colors.semantic.success.base};
        --color-warning: ${this.tokens.colors.semantic.warning.base};
        --color-error: ${this.tokens.colors.semantic.error.base};
        --color-info: ${this.tokens.colors.semantic.info.base};
        
        --color-bg-primary: ${this.tokens.colors.background.light.primary};
        --color-bg-secondary: ${this.tokens.colors.background.light.secondary};
        --color-bg-tertiary: ${this.tokens.colors.background.light.tertiary};
        --color-bg-overlay: ${this.tokens.colors.background.light.overlay};
        
        --color-text-primary: ${this.tokens.colors.text.light.primary};
        --color-text-secondary: ${this.tokens.colors.text.light.secondary};
        --color-text-tertiary: ${this.tokens.colors.text.light.tertiary};
        --color-text-disabled: ${this.tokens.colors.text.light.disabled};
        --color-text-inverse: ${this.tokens.colors.text.light.inverse};
        
        /* Typography Tokens */
        --font-family-primary: ${this.tokens.typography.fontFamily.primary};
        --font-family-mono: ${this.tokens.typography.fontFamily.mono};
        
        --font-size-xs: ${this.tokens.typography.fontSize.xs};
        --font-size-sm: ${this.tokens.typography.fontSize.sm};
        --font-size-base: ${this.tokens.typography.fontSize.base};
        --font-size-lg: ${this.tokens.typography.fontSize.lg};
        --font-size-xl: ${this.tokens.typography.fontSize.xl};
        --font-size-2xl: ${this.tokens.typography.fontSize['2xl']};
        --font-size-3xl: ${this.tokens.typography.fontSize['3xl']};
        
        --font-weight-regular: ${this.tokens.typography.fontWeight.regular};
        --font-weight-medium: ${this.tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium};
        --font-weight-semibold: ${this.tokens.typography.fontWeight.semibold};
        --font-weight-bold: ${this.tokens.typography.fontWeight.bold};
        
        --line-height-tight: ${this.tokens.typography.lineHeight.tight};
        --line-height-normal: ${this.tokens.typography.lineHeight.normal};
        --line-height-relaxed: ${this.tokens.typography.lineHeight.relaxed};
        
        /* Spacing Tokens */
        --spacing-0: ${this.tokens.spacing[0]};
        --spacing-1: ${this.tokens.spacing[1]};
        --spacing-2: ${this.tokens.spacing[2]};
        --spacing-3: ${this.tokens.spacing[3]};
        --spacing-4: ${this.tokens.spacing[4]};
        --spacing-5: ${this.tokens.spacing[5]};
        --spacing-6: ${this.tokens.spacing[6]};
        --spacing-7: ${this.tokens.spacing[7]};
        --spacing-8: ${this.tokens.spacing[8]};
        --spacing-9: ${this.tokens.spacing[9]};
        --spacing-10: ${this.tokens.spacing[10]};
        
        /* Border Radius Tokens */
        --radius-none: ${this.tokens.borderRadius.none};
        --radius-sm: ${this.tokens.borderRadius.sm};
        --radius-base: ${this.tokens.borderRadius.base};
        --radius-md: ${this.tokens.borderRadius.md};
        --radius-lg: ${this.tokens.borderRadius.lg};
        --radius-xl: ${this.tokens.borderRadius.xl};
        --radius-2xl: ${this.tokens.borderRadius['2xl']};
        --radius-full: ${this.tokens.borderRadius.full};
        
        /* Shadow Tokens */
        --shadow-sm: ${this.tokens.shadows.sm};
        --shadow-base: ${this.tokens.shadows.base};
        --shadow-md: ${this.tokens.shadows.md};
        --shadow-lg: ${this.tokens.shadows.lg};
        --shadow-xl: ${this.tokens.shadows.xl};
        --shadow-2xl: ${this.tokens.shadows['2xl']};
        --shadow-inner: ${this.tokens.shadows.inner};
        
        /* Animation Tokens */
        --animation-duration-fast: ${this.tokens.animation.duration.fast};
        --animation-duration-normal: ${this.tokens.animation.duration.normal};
        --animation-duration-slow: ${this.tokens.animation.duration.slow};
        
        --animation-easing-ease-in-out: ${this.tokens.animation.easing.easeInOut};
        --animation-easing-ease-out: ${this.tokens.animation.easing.easeOut};
        --animation-easing-ease-in: ${this.tokens.animation.easing.easeIn};
        --animation-easing-sharp: ${this.tokens.animation.easing.sharp};
        
        /* Theme Mode */
        --theme-mode: 'light';
      }
    `;
  }
  
  // Get CSS custom properties for dark mode
  getDarkModeCSS() {
    return `
      [data-theme="dark"] {
        /* Color Tokens - Dark Mode */
        --color-bg-primary: ${this.tokens.colors.background.dark.primary};
        --color-bg-secondary: ${this.tokens.colors.background.dark.secondary};
        --color-bg-tertiary: ${this.tokens.colors.background.dark.tertiary};
        --color-bg-overlay: ${this.tokens.colors.background.dark.overlay};
        
        --color-text-primary: ${this.tokens.colors.text.dark.primary};
        --color-text-secondary: ${this.tokens.colors.text.dark.secondary};
        --color-text-tertiary: ${this.tokens.colors.text.dark.tertiary};
        --color-text-disabled: ${this.tokens.colors.text.dark.disabled};
        --color-text-inverse: ${this.tokens.colors.text.dark.inverse};
        
        /* Shadow adjustments for dark mode */
        --shadow-sm: 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);
        --shadow-base: 0 1px 3px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3), 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
        --shadow-md: 0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
        --shadow-lg: 0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
        --shadow-xl: 0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
        
        /* Theme Mode */
        --theme-mode: 'dark';
      }
    `;
  }
  
  // Apply tokens to document
  applyTokens() {
    const style = document.createElement('style');
    style.textContent = this.getLightModeCSS() + this.getDarkModeCSS();
    document.head.appendChild(style);
  }
  
  // Toggle theme
  toggleTheme() {
    const html = document.documentElement;
    const currentTheme = html.getAttribute('data-theme');
    const newTheme = currentTheme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark';
    
    html.setAttribute('data-theme

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Serviços Backend

```
