## 4. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_v11
      POSTGRES_USER: postgres
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./src/database/migrations:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U postgres"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  app:
    build: .
    container_name: diyapp-core
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DB_HOST: postgres
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_NAME: diyapp_v11
      DB_USER: postgres
      DB_PASSWORD: postgres
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

## 5. Dockerfile

```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

COPY . .
RUN npm run build

FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

RUN apk add --no-cache tini

COPY --from=builder /app/package*.json ./
COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder /app/src/database/migrations ./src/database/migrations
COPY --from=builder /app/public ./public

USER node

ENTRYPOINT ["/sbin/tini", "--"]
CMD ["node", "dist/index.js"]
```

## 6. src/index.ts

```typescript
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import compression from 'compression';
import { config } from './config';
import { logger } from './utils/logger';
import { errorHandler } from './middleware/errorHandler';
import { rateLimiter } from './middleware/rateLimiter';
import { metricsMiddleware, metricsEndpoint } from './utils/metrics';
import { initializeDatabase } from './database';
import { setupSwagger } from './docs/swagger';

// Import routers
import orchestratorRouter from './services/orchestrator/orchestrator.router';
import auditRouter from './services/audit/audit.router';
import healthRouter from './services/health/health.router';

const app = express();
const PORT = config.port;

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: config.corsOrigin,
  credentials: true
}));

// Compression
app.use(compression());

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Metrics middleware
app.use(metricsMiddleware);

// Rate limiting for public endpoints
app.use('/api/v1/public', rateLimiter);

// Health endpoint (no auth required)
app.use('/health', healthRouter);

// API Documentation
setupSwagger(app);

// API Routes
app.use(`/api/${config.apiVersion}/orchestrator`, orchestratorRouter);
app.use(`/api/${config.apiVersion}/audit`, auditRouter);
app.use(`/api/${config.apiVersion}/health`, healthRouter);

// Public dashboard
app.use(express.static('public'));

// Error handling (must be last)
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start server
async function startServer() {
  try {
    // Initialize database
    await initializeDatabase();
    logger.info('Database initialized successfully');

    // Start server
    app.listen(PORT, () => {
      logger.info(`Server running on port ${PORT}`);
      logger.info(`Environment: ${config.nodeEnv}`);
      logger.info(`API Version: ${config.apiVersion}`);
      logger.info(`Metrics available at /metrics`);
      logger.info(`API Docs available at /api-docs`);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to start server:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

// Handle uncaught errors
process.on('uncaughtException', (error) => {
  logger.error('Uncaught Exception:', error);
  process.exit(1);
});

process.on('unhandledRejection', (reason, promise) => {
  logger.error('Unhandled Rejection at:', promise, 'reason:', reason);
});

startServer();
```

## 7. src/config/index.ts

```typescript
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import Joi from 'joi';

dotenv.config();

const envSchema = Joi.object({
  NODE_ENV: Joi.string()
    .valid('development', 'production', 'test')
    .default('development'),
  
  PORT: Joi.number()
    .default(3000),
  
  API_VERSION: Joi.string()
    .default('v1'),
  
  DB_HOST: Joi.string()
    .default('localhost'),
  
  DB_PORT: Joi.number()
    .default(5432),
  
  DB_NAME: Joi.string()
    .required(),
  
  DB_USER: Joi.string()
    .required(),
  
  DB_PASSWORD: Joi.string()
    .required(),
  
  DB_POOL_MAX: Joi.number()
    .default(20),
  
  DB_SSL: Joi.boolean()
    .default(false),
  
  JWT_SECRET: Joi.string()
    .required()
    .min(32),
  
  JWT_EXPIRES_IN: Joi.string()
    .default('24h'),
  
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS: Joi.number()
    .default(900000),
  
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS: Joi.number()
    .default(100),
  
  CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD: Joi.number()
    .default(5),
  
  CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT: Joi.number()
    .default(30000),
  
  MAX_RETRIES: Joi.number()
    .default(3),
  
  RETRY_DELAY_MS: Joi.number()
    .default(1000),
  
  HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL: Joi.number()
    .default(30000),
  
  AGENT_TIMEOUT_MS: Joi.number()
    .default(5000),
  
  LOG_LEVEL: Joi.string()
    .valid('error', 'warn', 'info', 'debug')
    .default('info'),
  
  LOG_TO_FILE: Joi.boolean()
    .default(true),
  
  EXTERNAL_API_TIMEOUT: Joi.number()
    .default(10000),
  
  EXTERNAL_API_RETRIES: Joi.number()
    .default(2),
  
  CORS_ORIGIN: Joi.string()
    .default('*')
}).unknown();

const { error, value: envVars } = envSchema.validate(process.env);

if (error) {
  throw new Error(`Config validation error: ${error.message}`);
}

export const config = {
  nodeEnv: envVars.NODE_ENV,
  port: envVars.PORT,
  apiVersion: envVars.API_VERSION,
  
  database: {
    host: envVars.DB_HOST,
    port: envVars.DB_PORT,
    name: envVars.DB_NAME,
    user: envVars.DB_USER,
    password: envVars.DB_PASSWORD,
    poolMax: envVars.DB_POOL_MAX,
    ssl: envVars.DB_SSL
  },
  
  jwt: {
    secret: envVars.JWT_SECRET,
    expiresIn: envVars.JWT_EXPIRES_IN
  },
  
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: envVars.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS,
    maxRequests: envVars.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS
  },
  
  circuitBreaker: {
    threshold: envVars.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD,
    timeout: envVars.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT
  },
  
  retry: {
    maxRetries: envVars.MAX_RETRIES,
    delayMs: envVars.RETRY_DELAY_MS
  },
  
  healthCheck: {
    interval: envVars.HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL,
    agentTimeout: envVars.AGENT_TIMEOUT_MS
  },
  
  logging: {
    level: envVars.LOG_LEVEL,
    toFile: envVars.LOG_TO_FILE
  },
  
  externalApi: {
    timeout: envVars.EXTERNAL_API_TIMEOUT,
    retries: envVars.EXTERNAL_API_RETRIES
  },
  
  corsOrigin: envVars.CORS_ORIGIN
};
```

## 8. src/database/index.ts

```typescript
import { Pool, PoolConfig } from 'pg';
import { config } from '../config';
import { logger } from '../utils/logger';

const poolConfig: PoolConfig = {
  host: config.database.host,
  port: config.database.port,
  database: config.database.name,
  user: config.database.user,
  password: config.database.password,
  max: config.database.poolMax,
  idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
  connectionTimeoutMillis: 2000,
  ssl: config.database.ssl ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false
};

export const pool = new Pool(poolConfig);

// Test database connection
pool.on('connect', () => {
  logger.debug('Database connection established');
});

pool.on('error', (err) => {
  logger.error('Unexpected database error:', err);
  process.exit(-1);
});

export const initializeDatabase = async (): Promise<void> => {
  try {
    // Test connection
    const client = await pool.connect();
    
    // Check if tables exist
    const result = await client.query(`
      SELECT EXISTS (
        SELECT FROM information_schema.tables 
        WHERE table_schema = 'public' 
        AND table

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Telemetria e Métricas

## Estrutura do Projeto

## 1. Docker Compose para Infraestrutura

**docker-compose.yml**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # TimescaleDB (PostgreSQL com extensões de time-series)
  timescaledb:
    image: timescale/timescaledb:latest-pg15
    container_name: diyapp_timescaledb
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_telemetry
      POSTGRES_USER: telemetry_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${TIMESCALEDB_PASSWORD}
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - timescaledb_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./src/data/schemas:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    command: >
      postgres
      -c shared_preload_libraries=timescaledb
      -c max_connections=200
      -c shared_buffers=1GB
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U telemetry_user -d diyapp_telemetry"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Airflow para orquestração
  airflow:
    image: apache/airflow:2.7.1
    container_name: diyapp_airflow
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
      AIRFLOW__DATABASE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow_user:${AIRFLOW_DB_PASSWORD}@airflow_db:5432/airflow
      AIRFLOW__CORE__LOAD_EXAMPLES: 'false'
      AIRFLOW__WEBSERVER__SECRET_KEY: ${AIRFLOW_SECRET_KEY}
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./airflow/logs:/opt/airflow/logs
      - ./airflow/plugins:/opt/airflow/plugins
    depends_on:
      airflow_db:
        condition: service_healthy
      timescaledb:
        condition: service_healthy
    command: >
      bash -c "
      airflow db init &&
      airflow users create --username admin --firstname Admin --lastname User --role Admin --email admin@diyapp.com --password ${AIRFLOW_ADMIN_PASSWORD} &&
      airflow webserver & airflow scheduler
      "

  # Banco de dados do Airflow
  airflow_db:
    image: postgres:13
    container_name: diyapp_airflow_db
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: airflow
      POSTGRES_USER: airflow_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${AIRFLOW_DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - airflow_db_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U airflow_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Metabase para visualização
  metabase:
    image: metabase/metabase:latest
    container_name: diyapp_metabase
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      MB_DB_TYPE: postgres
      MB_DB_DBNAME: metabase
      MB_DB_PORT: 5432
      MB_DB_USER: metabase_user
      MB_DB_PASS: ${METABASE_DB_PASSWORD}
      MB_DB_HOST: metabase_db
    depends_on:
      metabase_db:
        condition: service_healthy
      timescaledb:
        condition: service_healthy

  # Banco de dados do Metabase
  metabase_db:
    image: postgres:13
    container_name: diyapp_metabase_db
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: metabase
      POSTGRES_USER: metabase_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${METABASE_DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - metabase_db_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U metabase_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

volumes:
  timescaledb_data:
  airflow_db_data:
  metabase_db_data:

## 2. Schema de Dados para Telemetria

**src/data/schemas/telemetry_schema.sql**
```sql
-- Schema principal para telemetria DIYAPP V11
-- Camada RAW (bronze) - dados brutos preservados

-- Tabela de eventos brutos do sistema
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_telemetry_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    event_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    device_info JSONB,
    event_data JSONB NOT NULL,
    source_system VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    received_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    processed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
);

-- Criar índice para queries por tempo
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_telemetry_timestamp ON raw_telemetry_events (event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_telemetry_type ON raw_telemetry_events (event_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_telemetry_processed ON raw_telemetry_events (processed);

-- Tabela de métricas de performance LLM
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_llm_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuiduid(),
    request_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    request_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    response_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    
    -- Métricas de tempo
    total_duration_ms INTEGER NOT NULL,
    tokenization_duration_ms INTEGER,
    inference_duration_ms INTEGER,
    network_latency_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Métricas de tokens
    prompt_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    completion_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (prompt_tokens + completion_tokens) STORED,
    
    -- Métricas de custo
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    cost_currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT 'USD',
    
    -- Métricas de qualidade
    accuracy_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    confidence_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    error_code VARCHAR(50),
    error_message TEXT,
    
    -- Metadados
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    environment VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'production',
    tags JSONB,
    
    -- Controle de pipeline
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    batch_id VARCHAR(100)
);

-- Criar índice para queries de performance
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_metrics_timestamp ON raw_llm_metrics (request_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_metrics_model ON raw_llm_metrics (model_name, provider);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_metrics_feature ON raw_llm_metrics (feature_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_metrics_duration ON raw_llm_metrics (total_duration_ms);

-- Habilitar extensão TimescaleDB
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS timescaledb;

-- Transformar tabelas em hypertables para otimização de time-series
SELECT create_hypertable('raw_telemetry_events', 'event_timestamp', 
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '1 day',
    if_not_exists => TRUE);

SELECT create_hypertable('raw_llm_metrics', 'request_timestamp',
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '1 day',
    if_not_exists => TRUE);

-- Tabela de agregações diárias (camada marts)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mart_performance_daily (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Agregações de volume
    total_requests BIGINT NOT NULL,
    successful_requests BIGINT NOT NULL,
    failed_requests BIGINT NOT NULL,
    
    -- Agregações de tempo (percentis)
    p50_duration_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p90_duration_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p95_duration_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p99_duration_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    avg_duration_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    max_duration_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Agregações de tokens
    total_prompt_tokens BIGINT,
    total_completion_tokens BIGINT,
    avg_prompt_tokens DECIMAL(10,2),
    avg_completion_tokens DECIMAL(10,2),
    
    -- Agregações de custo
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(15,6),
    avg_cost_per_request DECIMAL(10,6),
    
    -- Agregações de qualidade
    avg_accuracy_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    avg_confidence_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    
    -- Metadados
    computed_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, model_name, provider, feature_name)
);

-- Tabela de tendências de acurácia
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mart_accuracy_trends (
    trend_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    model_version VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    evaluation_date DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Métricas de avaliação
    accuracy_score DECIMAL(5,4) NOT NULL,
    precision_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    recall_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    f1_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    
    -- Detalhes do dataset de avaliação
    evaluation_dataset_size INTEGER,
    evaluation_duration_seconds INTEGER,
    
    -- Comparação com baseline
    accuracy_delta DECIMAL(5,4),
    is_improvement BOOLEAN,
    
    -- Metadados
    evaluated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    evaluator VARCHAR(100),
    
    UNIQUE(feature_name, model_version, evaluation_date)
);

-- Tabela de alertas de qualidade
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS quality_alerts (
    alert_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    alert_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    severity VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (severity IN ('LOW', 'MEDIUM', 'HIGH', 'CRITICAL')),
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_value DECIMAL(15,6),
    threshold_value DECIMAL(15,6),
    
    -- Contexto
    model_name VARCHAR(100),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    time_window VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Status
    alert_status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'OPEN' CHECK (alert_status IN ('OPEN', 'ACKNOWLEDGED', 'RESOLVED', 'SUPPRESSED')),
    detected_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    acknowledged_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Detalhes
    description TEXT,
    suggested_action TEXT,
    
    -- Relacionamentos
    related_incident_id VARCHAR(100)
);

-- Criar índices para queries de alertas
CREATE INDEX idx_quality_alerts_status ON quality_alerts (alert_status, severity);
CREATE INDEX idx_quality_alerts_detected ON quality_alerts (detected_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_quality_alerts_metric ON quality_alerts (metric_name, model_name);

-- View para dashboard de performance em tempo real
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW vw_realtime_performance AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('hour', request_timestamp) as hour_bucket,
    model_name,
    provider,
    feature_name,
    COUNT(*) as request_count,
    AVG(total_duration_ms) as avg_response_time,
    PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY total_duration_ms) as p95_response_time,
    SUM(total_tokens) as total_tokens_used,
    AVG(accuracy_score) as avg_accuracy,
    SUM(CASE WHEN error_code IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*) as success_rate
FROM raw_llm_metrics
WHERE request_timestamp >= NOW() - INTERVAL '24 hours'
GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
ORDER BY 1 DESC, request_count DESC;

-- View para análise de custo por feature
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW vw_cost_analysis AS
SELECT
    DATE(request_timestamp) as date,
    feature_name,
    model_name,
    provider,
    COUNT(*) as total_requests,
    SUM(total_tokens) as total_tokens,
    SUM(cost_usd) as total_cost,
    AVG(cost_usd) as avg_cost_per_request,
    SUM(total_tokens) / NULLIF(SUM(cost_usd), 0) as tokens_per_usd
FROM raw_llm_metrics
WHERE cost_usd IS NOT NULL AND cost_usd > 0
GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
ORDER BY 1 DESC, total_cost DESC;

-- Função para limpeza automática de dados antigos (retenção de 90 dias)
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION cleanup_old_telemetry_data(retention_days INTEGER DEFAULT 90)
RETURNS INTEGER AS $$
DECLARE
    deleted_count INTEGER;
BEGIN
    -- Limpar dados brutos antigos
    DELETE FROM raw_telemetry_events 
    WHERE event_timestamp < NOW() - (retention_days || ' days')::INTERVAL
    AND processed = TRUE;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS deleted_count = ROW_COUNT;
    
    -- Limpar métricas LLM antigas
    DELETE FROM raw_llm_metrics 
    WHERE request_timestamp < NOW() - (retention_days || ' days')::INTERVAL;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS deleted_count = deleted_count + ROW_COUNT;
    
    RETURN deleted_count;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Agendar limpeza automática (executar diariamente às 02:00)
SELECT add_job(
    'SELECT cleanup_old_telemetry_data(90);',
    '24 hours',
    'cleanup_old_telemetry'
);
```

## 3. Modelos de Dados Python

**src/data/models/telemetry.py**
```python
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, validator
from enum import Enum
import uuid

class Environment(str, Enum):
    PRODUCTION = "production"
    STAGING = "staging"
    DEVELOPMENT = "development"
    TESTING = "testing"

class EventType(str, Enum):
    LLM_REQUEST = "llm_request"
    LLM_RESPONSE = "llm_response"
    USER_INTERACTION = "user_interaction"
    SYSTEM_ERROR = "system_error"
    PERFORMANCE_METRIC = "performance_metric"
    COST_UPDATE = "cost_update"
    MODEL_DEPLOYMENT = "model_deployment"

class TelemetryEvent(BaseModel):
    """Modelo para eventos de telemetria brutos"""
    event_id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    event_type: EventType
    event_timestamp: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    session_id: Optional[str] = None
    user_id: Optional[str] = None
    app_version: str = "v11.0.0"
    device_info: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    event_data: Dict[str, Any]
    source_system: str = "diyapp_core"
    
    class Config:
        json_encoders = {
            datetime: lambda dt: dt.isoformat()
        }

class LLMMetric(BaseModel):
    """Modelo para métricas de performance LL

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura Técnica

## 1. DECISÕES ARQUITETURAIS (ADRs)

### ADR-001: Stack Tecnológica Principal
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
Precisamos definir uma stack tecnológica moderna, produtiva e com bom ecossistema para uma aplicação autônoma que requer estabilidade, escalabilidade e facilidade de manutenção.

**DECISÃO:**
- **Frontend:** React 18 + TypeScript + Vite
- **Backend:** Node.js 20 + Express + TypeScript
- **Banco de Dados:** PostgreSQL (produção) + SQLite (desenvolvimento/testes)
- **Cache:** Redis
- **Fila de Mensagens:** Bull (Redis-based)
- **Containerização:** Docker + Docker Compose
- **Orquestração:** Kubernetes (preparação)
- **CI/CD:** GitHub Actions
- **Monitoramento:** Prometheus + Grafana + Winston (logs)

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A (Vue.js + Go):** Vue.js para front, Go para back
  - Prós: Performance excelente no backend, Vue mais simples que React
  - Contras: Ecossistema menor para Go, curva de aprendizado para time full-stack
- **Opção B (React + Node.js):** React para front, Node.js para back
  - Prós: Ecossistema vasto, TypeScript em ambos, produtividade alta, fácil contratação
  - Contras: Node.js single-threaded (mitigável com clusters)
- **Escolhida:** Opção B - Justificativa: Produtividade, consistência de linguagem, vasto ecossistema, adequado para MVP rápido com estabilidade

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
- Positivas: Desenvolvimento rápido, code sharing entre front/back, ampla documentação
- Negativas: Performance CPU-intensive limitada no Node.js
- Riscos: Callback hell (mitigado com async/await), memory leaks (mitigado com monitoring)

### ADR-002: Estrutura de Pastas
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
Necessidade de estrutura escalável que suporte múltiplas squads trabalhando em paralelo (Modo Hive) sem conflitos.

**DECISÃO:**
```
diyapp-v11/
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/          # CI/CD pipelines
├── apps/
│   ├── web/               # Frontend React app
│   ├── api/               # Backend Node.js API
│   └── worker/            # Background jobs processor
├── packages/
│   ├── shared/           # Código compartilhado TypeScript
│   ├── database/         # Database models/migrations
│   └── utils/            # Utilities compartilhadas
├── infrastructure/
│   ├── docker/           # Docker configs
│   ├── k8s/              # Kubernetes manifests
│   └── monitoring/       # Prometheus/Grafana configs
├── docs/
│   ├── adrs/             # Architecture Decision Records
│   └── api/              # API documentation
└── scripts/              # Build/deploy scripts
```

### ADR-003: Estratégia de Deploy
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

**DECISÃO:**
- **Ambientes:** dev → staging → production
- **Deploy:** Blue-Green para API, Canary para frontend
- **Rollback:** Automático em caso de health check failures
- **Database Migrations:** Flyway, executadas antes do deploy da app

### 2.4 apps/web/src/main.tsx
```tsx
import React from 'react'
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom/client'
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query'
import { ReactQueryDevtools } from '@tanstack/react-query-devtools'
import App from './App'
import './index.css'

// Create a client
const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: {
      staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
      retry: 2,
      refetchOnWindowFocus: false,
    },
  },
})

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById('root')!).render(
  <React.StrictMode>
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      <App />
      <ReactQueryDevtools initialIsOpen={false} />
    </QueryClientProvider>
  </React.StrictMode>,
)
```

### 2.5 apps/web/src/App.tsx
```tsx
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { Toaster } from 'react-hot-toast'
import Dashboard from './pages/Dashboard'
import Tasks from './pages/Tasks'
import Monitoring from './pages/Monitoring'
import Settings from './pages/Settings'
import Layout from './components/Layout'
import { SystemStatusProvider } from './contexts/SystemStatusContext'

function App() {
  return (
    <SystemStatusProvider>
      <Router>
        <Layout>
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
            <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="/tasks" element={<Tasks />} />
            <Route path="/monitoring" element={<Monitoring />} />
            <Route path="/settings" element={<Settings />} />
            <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
          </Routes>
        </Layout>
        <Toaster 
          position="top-right"
          toastOptions={{
            duration: 4000,
            style: {
              background: '#363636',
              color: '#fff',
            },
            success: {
              duration: 3000,
              iconTheme: {
                primary: '#10b981',
                secondary: '#fff',
              },
            },
            error: {
              duration: 5000,
              iconTheme: {
                primary: '#ef4444',
                secondary: '#fff',
              },
            },
          }}
        />
      </Router>
    </SystemStatusProvider>
  )
}

export default App
```

### 2.6 apps/web/src/pages/Dashboard.tsx
```tsx
import React from 'react'
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query'
import { 
  Activity, 
  Cpu, 
  Database, 
  Shield, 
  Zap,
  AlertCircle,
  CheckCircle2,
  Clock
} from 'lucide-react'
import StatCard from '../components/StatCard'
import SystemHealth from '../components/SystemHealth'
import RecentActivity from '../components/RecentActivity'
import { api } from '../lib/api'

const Dashboard: React.FC = () => {
  const { data: stats, isLoading } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['dashboard-stats'],
    queryFn: () => api.get('/api/v1/dashboard/stats'),
    refetchInterval: 30000, // 30 seconds
  })

  const { data: activities } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['recent-activities'],
    queryFn: () => api.get('/api/v1/activities/recent'),
    refetchInterval: 60000, // 1 minute
  })

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900">Squad Dashboard</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-600">Monitoramento em tempo real da squad autônoma</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
          <div className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-sm font-medium ${
            stats?.systemStatus === 'healthy' 
              ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-800' 
              : 'bg-red-100 text-red-800'
          }`}>
            {stats?.systemStatus === 'healthy' ? (
              <CheckCircle2 className="inline w-4 h-4 mr-1" />
            ) : (
              <AlertCircle className="inline w-4 h-4 mr-1" />
            )}
            {stats?.systemStatus === 'healthy' ? 'Operacional' : 'Degradado'}
          </div>
          <Clock className="w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
          <span className="text-sm text-gray-500">
            {new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Stats Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
        <StatCard
          title="Tarefas Ativas"
          value={stats?.activeTasks || 0}
          change="+12%"
          icon={<Activity className="w-6 h-6" />}
          color="blue"
          loading={isLoading}
        />
        <StatCard
          title="CPU Usage"
          value={`${stats?.cpuUsage || 0}%`}
          change="-3%"
          icon={<Cpu className="w-6 h-6" />}
          color="green"
          loading={isLoading}
        />
        <StatCard
          title="DB Connections"
          value={stats?.dbConnections || 0}
          change="+5%"
          icon={<Database className="w-6 h-6" />}
          color="purple"
          loading={isLoading}
        />
        <StatCard
          title="Response Time"
          value={`${stats?.avgResponseTime || 0}ms`}
          change="-15ms"
          icon={<Zap className="w-6 h-6" />}
          color="yellow"
          loading={isLoading}
        />
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        <div className="lg:col-span-2">
          <SystemHealth />
        </div>
        <div>
          <RecentActivity activities={activities?.slice(0, 5) || []} />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Security Status */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
        <div className="flex items-center mb-4">
          <Shield className="w-6 h-6 text-green-600 mr-2" />
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">Status de Segurança</h2>
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
            <span className="text-gray-700">Autenticação</span>
            <span className="px-2 py-1 bg-green-100 text-green-800 text-sm rounded">Ativa</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
            <span className="text-gray-700">Rate Limiting</span>
            <span className="px-2 py-1 bg-green-100 text-green-800 text-sm rounded">Configurado</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
            <span className="text-gray-700">Vulnerabilidades</span>
            <span className="px-2 py-1 bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 text-sm rounded">0 críticas</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

export default Dashboard
```

    "test": "vitest",
    "test:coverage": "vitest run --coverage",
    "db:migrate": "node -r ts-node/register ./node_modules/.bin/flyway migrate",
    "db:seed": "node -r ts-node/register ./scripts/seed.ts"

```javascript
// src/server.js
require('dotenv').config();
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const winston = require('winston');
const expressWinston = require('express-winston');
const { initializeDatabase } = require('./db/connection');
const { errorHandler } = require('./middleware/error-handler');
const { requestId } = require('./middleware/request-id');
const apiRoutes = require('./routes/api');
const graphqlRoutes = require('./routes/graphql');
const swaggerRoutes = require('./routes/swagger');
const healthRoutes = require('./routes/health');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || '*',
  credentials: true
}));

// Rate limiting for public endpoints
const publicLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
  message: { error: 'Too many requests, please try again later.' },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
});
app.use('/api/public', publicLimiter);

// Request ID middleware
app.use(requestId);

// Structured logging middleware
app.use(expressWinston.logger({
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/access.log' })
  ],
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  meta: true,
  msg: 'HTTP {{req.method}} {{req.url}}',
  expressFormat: true,
  colorize: false,
  ignoreRoute: (req, res) => req.path === '/health'
}));

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Routes
app.use('/health', healthRoutes);
app.use('/api-docs', swaggerRoutes);
app.use('/api', apiRoutes);
app.use('/graphql', graphqlRoutes);

// Error handling middleware (must be last)
app.use(expressWinston.errorLogger({
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log' })
  ],
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  )
}));
app.use(errorHandler);

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  console.log('SIGTERM received. Starting graceful shutdown...');
  server.close(() => {
    console.log('HTTP server closed.');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

// Initialize and start server
async function startServer() {
  try {
    await initializeDatabase();
    
    const server = app.listen(PORT, () => {
      console.log(`Server running on port ${PORT}`);
      console.log(`API Documentation: http://localhost:${PORT}/api-docs`);
      console.log(`GraphQL Playground: http://localhost:${PORT}/graphql`);
    });

    // Set timeout to prevent hanging connections
    server.keepAliveTimeout = 65000;
    server.headersTimeout = 66000;

    return server;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to start server:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

// Only start server if this file is run directly
if (require.main === module) {
  startServer();
}

module.exports = { app, startServer };
```

```javascript
// src/db/connection.js
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const winston = require('winston');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: winston.format.json(),
  transports: [new winston.transports.Console()]
});

class DatabaseConnection {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
    this.retryCount = 0;
    this.maxRetries = 3;
  }

  async connect() {
    const config = {
      host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: process.env.DB_PORT || 5432,
      database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v11',
      user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
      password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
      max: 20, // max number of clients in the pool
      idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: 5000,
    };

    this.pool = new Pool(config);

    // Test connection
    try {
      const client = await this.pool.connect();
      const result = await client.query('SELECT NOW()');
      client.release();
      
      this.isConnected = true;
      logger.info('Database connected successfully');
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Database connection failed:', error);
      
      if (this.retryCount < this.maxRetries) {
        this.retryCount++;
        logger.info(`Retrying database connection (attempt ${this.retryCount}/${this.maxRetries})...`);
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000 * this.retryCount));
        return this.connect();
      }
      
      throw new Error(`Failed to connect to database after ${this.maxRetries} attempts`);
    }
  }

  async query(text, params) {
    if (!this.isConnected) {
      throw new Error('Database not connected');
    }

    const start = Date.now();
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.debug('Query executed', {
        query: text,
        duration,
        rowCount: result.rowCount
      });
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Query failed:', {
        query: text,
        params: this.maskSensitiveData(params),
        error: error.message
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  maskSensitiveData(params) {
    if (!params) return params;
    
    const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'secret', 'key', 'credit_card'];
    return params.map(param => {
      if (typeof param === 'string') {
        for (const field of sensitiveFields) {
          if (param.toLowerCase().includes(field)) {
            return '[MASKED]';
          }
        }
      }
      return param;
    });
  }

  async disconnect() {
    if (this.pool) {
      await this.pool.end();
      this.isConnected = false;
      logger.info('Database disconnected');
    }
  }

  async getClient() {
    if (!this.isConnected) {
      throw new Error('Database not connected');
    }
    return await this.pool.connect();
  }
}

const db = new DatabaseConnection();

async function initializeDatabase() {
  await db.connect();
  
  // Run migrations
  const { runMigrations } = require('./migrations/run-migrations');
  await runMigrations('up');
  
  return db;
}

module.exports = { db, initializeDatabase };
```

```javascript
// src/db/models/user.js
const { db } = require('../connection');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class User {
  static async create({ email, password, name, role = 'user' }) {
    const userId = uuidv4();
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    const now = new Date().toISOString();

    const query = `
      INSERT INTO users (id, email, password_hash, name, role, created_at, updated_at)
      VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7)
      RETURNING id, email, name, role, created_at, updated_at
    `;

    const result = await db.query(query, [
      userId, email, hashedPassword, name, role, now, now
    ]);

    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async findByEmail(email) {
    const query = 'SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = $1';
    const result = await db.query(query, [email]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async findById(id) {
    const query = 'SELECT id, email, name, role, created_at, updated_at FROM users WHERE id = $1';
    const result = await db.query(query, [id]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async update(id, updates) {
    const allowedUpdates = ['name', 'email', 'role'];
    const updateFields = [];
    const values = [];
    let paramCount = 1;

    for (const [field, value] of Object.entries(updates)) {
      if (allowedUpdates.includes(field)) {
        updateFields.push(`${field} = $${paramCount}`);
        values.push(value);
        paramCount++;
      }
    }

    if (updateFields.length === 0) {
      throw new Error('No valid fields to update');
    }

    updateFields.push(`updated_at = $${paramCount}`);
    values.push(new Date().toISOString());
    paramCount++;

    values.push(id);

    const query = `
      UPDATE users 
      SET ${updateFields.join(', ')}
      WHERE id = $${paramCount}
      RETURNING id, email, name, role, created_at, updated_at
    `;

    const result = await db.query(query, values);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async verifyPassword(user, password) {
    return await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password_hash);
  }

  static async delete(id) {
    const query = 'DELETE FROM users WHERE id = $1 RETURNING id';
    const result = await db.query(query, [id]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async list({ page = 1, limit = 20, role } = {}) {
    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;
    let query = 'SELECT id, email, name, role, created_at, updated_at FROM users';
    const values = [];
    let paramCount = 1;

    if (role) {
      query += ` WHERE role = $${paramCount}`;
      values.push(role);
      paramCount++;
    }

    query += ` ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT $${paramCount} OFFSET $${paramCount + 1}`;
    values.push(limit, offset);

    const result = await db.query(query, values);
    return result.rows;
  }
}

module.exports = User;
```

```javascript
// src/db/models/project.js
const { db } = require('../connection');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class Project {
  static async create({ name, description, created_by }) {
    const projectId = uuidv4();
    const now = new Date().toISOString();

    const query = `
      INSERT INTO projects (id, name, description, created_by, created_at, updated_at)
      VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6)
      RETURNING *
    `;

    const result = await db.query(query, [
      projectId, name, description, created_by, now, now
    ]);

    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async findById(id) {
    const query = 'SELECT * FROM projects WHERE id = $1';
    const result = await db.query(query, [id]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async update(id, updates, userId) {
    const allowedUpdates = ['name', 'description', 'status'];
    const updateFields = [];
    const values = [];
    let paramCount = 1;

    for (const [field, value] of Object.entries(updates)) {
      if (allowedUpdates.includes(field)) {
        updateFields.push(`${field} = $${paramCount}`);
        values.push(value);
        paramCount++;
      }
    }

    if (updateFields.length === 0) {
      throw new Error('No valid fields to update');
    }

    updateFields.push(`updated_at = $${paramCount}`);
    values.push(new Date().toISOString());
    paramCount++;

    values.push(id);

    // Check ownership
    const ownershipCheck = 'SELECT created_by FROM projects WHERE id = $1';
    const ownershipResult = await db.query(ownershipCheck, [id]);
    
    if (ownershipResult.rows[0].created_by !== userId) {
      throw new Error('Not authorized to update this project');
    }

    const query = `
      UPDATE projects 
      SET ${updateFields.join(', ')}
      WHERE id = $${paramCount}
      RETURNING *
    `;

    const result = await db.query(query, values);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async delete(id, userId) {
    // Check ownership
    const ownershipCheck = 'SELECT created_by FROM projects WHERE id = $1';
    const ownershipResult = await db.query(ownershipCheck, [id]);
    
    if (!ownershipResult.rows[0]) {
      throw new Error('Project not found');
    }
    
    if (ownershipResult.rows[0].created_by !== userId) {
      throw new Error('Not authorized to delete this project');
    }

    const query = 'DELETE FROM projects WHERE id = $1 RETURNING id';
    const result = await db.query(query, [id]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  static async list({ page = 1, limit = 20, userId, status } = {}) {
    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;
    let query = 'SELECT * FROM projects';
    const values = [];
    let paramCount = 1;

    const conditions = [];
    
    if (userId) {
      conditions.push(`created_by = $${paramCount}`);
      values.push(userId);
      paramCount++;
    }
    
    if (status) {
      conditions.push(`status = $${paramCount}`);
      values.push(status);
      paramCount++;
    }

    if (conditions.length > 0) {
      query += ` WHERE ${conditions.join(' AND ')}`;
    }

    query += ` ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT $${paramCount} OFFSET $${paramCount + 1}`;
    values.push(limit, offset);

    const result = await db.query(query, values);
    return result.rows;
  }

  static async addMember(projectId, userId, role = 'member') {
    const query = `
      INSERT INTO project_members (project_id, user_id, role, joined_at)
      VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4)
      ON CONFLICT (project_id, user_id) 
      DO UPDATE SET role = $3, joined_at = $4
      RETURNING *
    `;

    const result = await db.query(query, [
      projectId, userId, role, new Date().toISOString()
    ]);

    return result.rows[0];
  }
}

module.exports = Project;
```

```javascript
// src/middleware/auth.js
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const ApiKey = require('../db/models/api-key');

const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-secret-key-change-in-production';
const JWT_EXPIRY = process.env.JWT_EXPIRY || '24h';

class AuthError extends Error {
  constructor(message, code = 401) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'AuthError';
    this.statusCode = code;
  }
}

async function authenticate(req, res, next) {
  try {
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
    
    if (!authHeader) {
      throw new AuthError('No authorization header');
    }

    const [scheme, token] = authHeader.split(' ');

    if (scheme.toLowerCase() !== 'bearer') {
      throw new AuthError('Invalid authentication scheme');
    }

    if (!token) {
      throw new AuthError('No token provided');
    }

    // Try JWT first
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      req.user = decoded;
      req.auth

## 1. Esquema de Banco de Dados Otimizado

### `database/migrations/001_initial_schema.sql`

```sql
-- DIYAPP V11 Core - Schema Principal
-- PostgreSQL 14+ com otimizações para performance e escalabilidade

-- Enable extensions
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "pg_stat_statements";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "pg_partman" SCHEMA partman;

-- Core tables with partitioning strategy
CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    hashed_password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    avatar_url TEXT,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- Indexes for common queries
    CONSTRAINT valid_email CHECK (email ~* '^[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}$')
);

-- Partitioned table for user activities (time-based partitioning)
CREATE TABLE user_activities (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    activity_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    entity_type VARCHAR(50),
    entity_id UUID,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Create monthly partitions for current year and next year
CREATE TABLE user_activities_y2024m01 PARTITION OF user_activities
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-01-01') TO ('2024-02-01');

CREATE TABLE user_activities_y2024m02 PARTITION OF user_activities
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-02-01') TO ('2024-03-01');

-- Projects table with GIN index for tags
CREATE TABLE projects (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(300) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    content JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
    tags TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    visibility VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'private' CHECK (visibility IN ('private', 'public', 'unlisted')),
    is_template BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    view_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    like_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    fork_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_activity_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- Full-text search vector
    search_vector tsvector GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        setweight(to_tsvector('english', coalesce(title, '')), 'A') ||
        setweight(to_tsvector('english', coalesce(description, '')), 'B')
    ) STORED
);

-- Comments with recursive structure for threads
CREATE TABLE comments (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    parent_id UUID REFERENCES comments(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    is_deleted BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- For efficient thread retrieval
    path UUID[] DEFAULT ARRAY[]::UUID[],
    depth INTEGER DEFAULT 0
);

-- Media storage metadata
CREATE TABLE media_files (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    filename VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    original_filename VARCHAR(255),
    mime_type VARCHAR(100),
    size_bytes BIGINT,
    storage_path TEXT NOT NULL,
    storage_provider VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'local',
    is_public BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    uploaded_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    CONSTRAINT positive_size CHECK (size_bytes > 0)
);

-- API keys for external integrations
CREATE TABLE api_keys (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    key_hash VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    last_four_chars CHAR(4) NOT NULL,
    scopes TEXT[] NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
    expires_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    last_used_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Audit log table (partitioned by month)
CREATE TABLE audit_logs (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    action VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    entity_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    entity_id UUID,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    old_values JSONB,
    new_values JSONB,
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Configuration table for system settings
CREATE TABLE system_config (
    key VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    value JSONB NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    is_public BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    updated_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);
```

### `database/migrations/002_add_audit_tables.sql`

```sql
-- DIYAPP V11 - Tabelas de Auditoria e Monitoramento

-- Performance metrics collection
CREATE TABLE performance_metrics (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    endpoint VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    method VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    status_code INTEGER,
    response_time_ms INTEGER NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    ip_address INET,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Database connection pool metrics
CREATE TABLE db_connection_metrics (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    total_connections INTEGER NOT NULL,
    active_connections INTEGER NOT NULL,
    idle_connections INTEGER NOT NULL,
    waiting_connections INTEGER NOT NULL,
    max_connections INTEGER NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Query performance analysis
CREATE TABLE slow_queries_log (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    query_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    execution_time_ms DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
    rows_returned INTEGER,
    parameters JSONB,
    plan JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- User sessions for analytics
CREATE TABLE user_sessions (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    session_token VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    device_info JSONB,
    ip_address INET,
    last_activity_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    expires_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Rate limiting tracking
CREATE TABLE rate_limit_log (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    ip_address INET NOT NULL,
    endpoint VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    request_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    window_start TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    window_end TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);
```

-- DIYAPP V11 - Índices de Performance Otimizados

-- Users table indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email_lower ON users(LOWER(email));
CREATE INDEX idx_users_username_lower ON users(LOWER(username));
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_last_login ON users(last_login_at DESC) WHERE last_login_at IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_users_active ON users(is_active) WHERE is_active = true;

-- Projects table indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_user_id ON projects(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_slug ON projects(slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_visibility ON projects(visibility) WHERE visibility = 'public';
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_created_at ON projects(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_updated_at ON projects(updated_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_last_activity ON projects(last_activity_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_view_count ON projects(view_count DESC) WHERE visibility = 'public';

-- GIN indexes for array and JSONB columns
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_tags ON projects USING GIN(tags);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_content ON projects USING GIN(content);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_search ON projects USING GIN(search_vector);

-- Comments table indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_project_id ON comments(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_user_id ON comments(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_parent_id ON comments(parent_id) WHERE parent_id IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_created_at ON comments(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_path ON comments USING GIN(path);
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_project_created ON comments(project_id, created_at DESC);

-- Media files indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_media_user_id ON media_files(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_media_uploaded_at ON media_files(uploaded_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_media_mime_type ON media_files(mime_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_media_metadata ON media_files USING GIN(metadata);

-- API keys indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_api_keys_user_id ON api_keys(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_api_keys_key_hash ON api_keys(key_hash);
CREATE INDEX idx_api_keys_expires ON api_keys(expires_at) WHERE expires_at IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_api_keys_active ON api_keys(is_active) WHERE is_active = true;

-- Activity tables indexes (partition-aware)
CREATE INDEX idx_user_activities_user_created ON user_activities(user_id, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_activities_type ON user_activities(activity_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_activities_entity ON user_activities(entity_type, entity_id) WHERE entity_id IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_user_activities_metadata ON user_activities USING GIN(metadata);

-- Audit logs indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_entity ON audit_logs(entity_type, entity_id) WHERE entity_id IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_user ON audit_logs(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_created ON audit_logs(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_action ON audit_logs(action);

-- Performance metrics indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_perf_metrics_endpoint ON performance_metrics(endpoint);
CREATE INDEX idx_perf_metrics_created ON performance_metrics(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_perf_metrics_response_time ON performance_metrics(response_time_ms DESC);

-- Session indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_user_sessions_token ON user_sessions(session_token);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_sessions_user ON user_sessions(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_sessions_expires ON user_sessions(expires_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_sessions_last_activity ON user_sessions(last_activity_at DESC);

-- Rate limit indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_rate_limit_ip ON rate_limit_log(ip_address, endpoint);
CREATE INDEX idx_rate_limit_user ON rate_limit_log(user_id, endpoint) WHERE user_id IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_rate_limit_window ON rate_limit_log(window_start, window_end);

-- Partial indexes for common query patterns
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_public_templates ON projects(is_template, visibility) 
    WHERE is_template = true AND visibility = 'public';

CREATE INDEX idx_comments_active ON comments(project_id, created_at DESC) 
    WHERE is_deleted = false;

CREATE INDEX idx_users_recently_active ON users(last_login_at DESC) 
    WHERE is_active = true AND last_login_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days';

-- BRIN indexes for large time-series tables
CREATE INDEX idx_brin_performance_metrics ON performance_metrics USING BRIN(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_brin_audit_logs ON audit_logs USING BRIN(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_brin_user_activities ON user_activities USING BRIN(created_at);
```

### `database/migrations/004_add_partitioning.sql`

```sql
-- DIYAPP V11 - Configuração de Particionamento Automático

-- Function to create monthly partitions automatically
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_monthly_partitions()
RETURNS void AS $$
DECLARE
    current_month DATE := DATE_TRUNC('month', NOW());
    next_month DATE := current_month + INTERVAL '1 month';
    partition_name TEXT;
    table_record RECORD;
BEGIN
    -- Tables to partition monthly
    FOR table_record IN 
        SELECT tablename 
        FROM pg_tables 
        WHERE schemaname = 'public' 
        AND tablename IN ('user_activities', 'audit_logs', 'performance_metrics')
    LOOP
        partition_name := table_record.tablename || '_y' || 
                         EXTRACT(YEAR FROM next_month) || 'm' || 
                         LPAD(EXTRACT(MONTH FROM next_month)::TEXT, 2, '0');
        
        -- Check if partition already exists
        IF NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_tables 
            WHERE schemaname = 'public' 
            AND tablename = partition_name
        ) THEN
            EXECUTE format(
                'CREATE TABLE %I PARTITION OF %I FOR VALUES FROM (%L) TO (%L)',
                partition_name,
                table_record.tablename,
                next_month,
                next_month + INTERVAL '1 month'
            );
            
            -- Create indexes on new partition
            EXECUTE format('CREATE INDEX ON %I (created_at DESC)', partition_name);
            
            RAISE NOTICE 'Created partition % for table %', partition_name, table_record.tablename;
        END IF;
    END LOOP;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Function to drop old partitions (keep 12 months)
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION drop_old_partitions()
RETURNS void AS $$
DECLARE
    partition_record RECORD;
    cutoff_date DATE := NOW() - INTERVAL '12 months';
BEGIN
    FOR partition_record IN 
        SELECT schemaname, tablename
        FROM pg_tables
        WHERE schemaname = 'public'
        AND tablename LIKE '%_y%m%'
        AND tablename ~ '^(user_activities|audit_logs|performance_metrics)_y\d{4}m\d{2}$'
    LOOP
        -- Extract date from partition name
        IF substring(partition_record.tablename from 'y(\d{4})m(\d{2})$') IS NOT NULL THEN
            DECLARE
                year_part INT := substring(partition_record.tablename from 'y(\d{4})')::INT;
                month_part INT := substring(partition_record.tablename from 'm(\d{2})$')::INT;
                partition_date DATE := MAKE_DATE(year_part, month_part, 1);
            BEGIN
                IF partition_date < cutoff_date THEN
                    EXECUTE format('DROP TABLE %I.%I', 
                        partition_record.schemaname, 
                        partition_record.tablename);
                    RAISE NOTICE 'Dropped old partition: %', partition_record.tablename;
                END IF;
            END;
        END IF;
    END LOOP;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Materialized view for dashboard metrics
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW dashboard_metrics AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('day', created_at) as metric_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as daily_active_users,
    COUNT(*) as total_activities,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN activity_type = 'login' THEN user_id END) as logins,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN activity_type = 'project_create' THEN user_id END) as project_creators
FROM user_activities
WHERE created_at >= NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days'
GROUP BY DATE_TRUNC('day', created_at)
WITH DATA;

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX idx_dashboard_metrics_date ON dashboard_metrics(metric_date);

-- Refresh function for materialized view
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION refresh_dashboard_metrics()
RETURNS void AS $$
BEGIN
    REFRESH MATERIALIZED VIEW CONCURRENTLY dashboard_metrics;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```javascript
// ============================================
// DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core Architecture
// Technical Architecture Specification v1.0
// ============================================

// ADR-001: Microservices Architecture Pattern
// Date: 2024-01-15
// Status: Accepted
// Authors: Tech Lead + Infra Specialist + Backend Lead

/**
 * CONTEXT:
 * DIYAPP V10 is a monolithic Node.js application that has become difficult to:
 * - Scale independently per component
 * - Deploy without full regression testing
 * - Maintain with multiple teams
 * - Isolate failures
 * 
 * FORCES:
 * - Need for independent scaling of AI processing vs API serving
 * - Requirement for 99.9% uptime per service
 * - Team autonomy in development and deployment
 * - Performance target: P95 latency < 200ms
 */

/**
 * DECISION:
 * Adopt microservices architecture with the following services:
 * 1. API Gateway Service (Node.js + Express)
 * 2. User Service (Node.js + TypeScript)
 * 3. AI Processing Service (Python + FastAPI)
 * 4. Notification Service (Node.js + BullMQ)
 * 5. Analytics Service (Go)
 * 
 * Each service:
 * - Owns its database/schema
 * - Communicates via gRPC for internal calls
 * - Exposes REST APIs for external calls (via Gateway)
 * - Has independent CI/CD pipeline
 * - Implements circuit breaker pattern
 */

/**
 * OPTIONS CONSIDERED:
 * - Option A: Monolithic with modules
 *   Pros: Simpler deployment, easier debugging
 *   Cons: No independent scaling, single point of failure
 * 
 * - Option B: Microservices with REST only
 *   Pros: Simpler communication, HTTP familiarity
 *   Cons: Higher latency, no streaming support
 * 
 * - Option C: Microservices with gRPC + REST
 *   Pros: Performance (binary protocol), streaming, type safety
 *   Cons: Learning curve, tooling complexity
 * 
 * Chosen: Option C - Justification: Performance requirements (P95 < 200ms)
 * necessitate binary protocol for internal service communication.
 */

/**
 * CONSEQUENCES:
 * Positive:
 * - Independent scaling per service
 * - Fault isolation
 * - Team autonomy
 * - Technology flexibility per service
 * 
 * Negative:
 * - Distributed tracing complexity
 * - Network latency between services
 * - Data consistency challenges
 * 
 * Risks:
 * - Network partition could break functionality
 * - Mitigation: Implement circuit breakers and fallbacks
 * - Service discovery failure
 * - Mitigation: Use Consul with health checks
 */

// ============================================
// Engineering Standards Document
// ============================================

const engineeringStandards = {
  version: "1.0",
  lastUpdated: "2024-01-15",
  
  // 1. Code Style & Formatting
  codeStyle: {
    language: "TypeScript",
    formatter: "Prettier",
    config: {
      semi: true,
      trailingComma: "es5",
      singleQuote: true,
      printWidth: 100,
      tabWidth: 2
    },
    linter: "ESLint",
    rules: {
      "no-unused-vars": "error",
      "no-console": ["warn", { allow: ["warn", "error"] }],
      "@typescript-eslint/explicit-function-return-type": "error"
    }
  },
  
  // 2. Git & Branching Strategy
  git: {
    branching: "GitFlow",
    branches: {
      main: "production code",
      develop: "integration branch",
      feature: "feature/*",
      release: "release/*",
      hotfix: "hotfix/*"
    },
    commits: "Conventional Commits",
    commitFormat: "<type>(<scope>): <description>",
    types: ["feat", "fix", "docs", "style", "refactor", "test", "chore"],
    scopeExamples: ["api", "auth", "ai", "notification"]
  },
  
  // 3. API Standards
  api: {
    external: {
      protocol: "REST",
      versioning: "URL path versioning (/api/v1/*)",
      authentication: "JWT Bearer tokens",
      rateLimiting: "Redis-based sliding window",
      documentation: "OpenAPI 3.0 (Swagger)"
    },
    internal: {
      protocol: "gRPC",
      versioning: "Protocol buffer package versioning",
      authentication: "mTLS with service certificates",
      timeout: "Default 5s, configurable per call"
    },
    errorFormat: {
      standard: {
        error: {
          code: "ERROR_CODE",
          message: "Human readable message",
          details: {},
          timestamp: "ISO8601"
        }
      }
    }
  },
  
  // 4. Performance Requirements
  performance: {
    latency: {
      p95: "200ms",
      p99: "500ms",
      timeout: "30s"
    },
    throughput: {
      requestsPerSecond: "1000+",
      concurrentConnections: "10000+"
    },
    resourceUsage: {
      maxMemory: "512MB per pod",
      maxCPU: "1 core per pod"
    }
  },
  
  // 5. Resilience Patterns
  resilience: {
    circuitBreaker: {
      implementation: "opossum",
      configuration: {
        timeout: 10000,
        errorThresholdPercentage: 50,
        resetTimeout: 30000,
        rollingCountTimeout: 10000,
        rollingCountBuckets: 10
      }
    },
    retry: {
      strategy: "exponential backoff",
      configuration: {
        retries: 3,
        factor: 2,
        minTimeout: 1000,
        maxTimeout: 10000,
        randomize: true
      }
    },
    bulkhead: {
      implementation: "bottleneck",
      configuration: {
        maxConcurrent: 10,
        minTime: 100
      }
    },
    fallback: "Required for all external service calls"
  },
  
  // 6. Testing Standards
  testing: {
    coverage: {
      minimum: 80,
      goal: 90
    },
    types: {
      unit: "Jest",
      integration: "Jest + Supertest",
      e2e: "Cypress",
      load: "k6"
    },
    requirements: {
      unit: "All business logic",
      integration: "All API endpoints",
      e2e: "Critical user journeys",
      load: "Performance requirements validation"
    }
  },
  
  // 7. Monitoring & Observability
  observability: {
    logging: {
      format: "JSON structured logs",
      levels: ["error", "warn", "info", "debug"],
      fields: ["timestamp", "level", "service", "correlationId", "userId", "message"]
    },
    metrics: {
      collection: "Prometheus",
      export: "/metrics endpoint",
      required: ["request_duration_seconds", "error_rate", "cpu_usage", "memory_usage"]
    },
    tracing: {
      implementation: "OpenTelemetry",
      sampling: "10% of requests",
      exporters: ["Jaeger", "Console"]
    },
    health: {
      endpoint: "/health",
      checks: ["database", "redis", "external_services"],
      response: {
        status: "up|down",
        timestamp: "ISO8601",
        checks: {}
      }
    }
  },
  
  // 8. Security Standards
  security: {
    authentication: "JWT with RS256",
    authorization: "RBAC with scopes",
    encryption: {
      atRest: "AES-256-GCM",
      inTransit: "TLS 1.3"
    },
    validation: {
      input: "Joi/Zod for all inputs",
      output: "Sanitize HTML/JS in responses"
    },
    headers: {
      required: [
        "X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff",
        "X-Frame-Options: DENY",
        "X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block"
      ]
    }
  },
  
  // 9. Deployment & Infrastructure
  deployment: {
    container: {
      baseImage: "node:18-alpine",
      multiStage: true,
      nonRootUser: true
    },
    orchestration: "Kubernetes",
    scaling: {
      horizontal: "HPA based on CPU/memory",
      vertical: "Resource limits per service"
    },
    config: {
      management: "Kubernetes ConfigMaps/Secrets",
      external: "HashiCorp Consul"
    }
  }
};

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <header>
            <h1>DIYAPP V11 - Service Dashboard</h1>
            <p class="subtitle">Microservices Architecture - Performance Target: P95 < 200ms</p>
        </header>
        
        <div class="alert" id="systemAlert" style="display: none;">
            <strong>System Alert:</strong> <span id="alertMessage"></span>
        </div>

            <!-- Services will be populated by JavaScript -->
        </div>
        
        <div class="controls">
            <button onclick="refreshAll()">Refresh All Services</button>
            <button onclick="runHealthChecks()">Run Health Checks</button>
            <button onclick="showPerformanceMetrics()">Performance Dashboard</button>
        </div>
        
        <footer>
            <p>DIYAPP V11 Core Architecture | Last Updated: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}</p>
            <p>Circuit Breaker Status: <span id="circuitStatus" class="status up"></span> Operational</p>
        </footer>
    </div>

    <script>
        const services = [
            { id: 'api-gateway', name: 'API Gateway', port: 3000, language: 'Node.js' },
            { id: 'user-service', name: 'User Service', port: 3001, language: 'TypeScript' },
            { id: 'ai-service', name: 'AI Processing', port: 8000, language: 'Python' },
            { id: 'notification-service', name: 'Notification', port: 3002, language: 'Node.js' },
            { id: 'analytics-service', name: 'Analytics', port: 8080, language: 'Go' }
        ];

        async function checkServiceHealth(service) {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(\`http://localhost:\${service.port}/health\`, {
                    signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000)
                });
                return await response.json();
            } catch (error) {
                return { status: 'down', error: error.message };
            }
        }

        function renderServices() {
            const grid = document.getElementById('servicesGrid');
            grid.innerHTML = '';
            
            services.forEach(service => {
                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'service-card';
                card.innerHTML = \`
                    <div class="service-name">
                        <span class="status" id="status-\${service.id}"></span>
                        \${service.name}
                    </div>
                    <p>Port: \${service.port} | Language: \${service.language}</p>
                    <div class="metrics">
                        <div class="metric">
                            <div class="metric-label">Latency (P95)</div>
                            <div class="metric-value" id="latency-\${service.id}">-- ms</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="metric">
                            <div class="metric-label">Error Rate</div>
                            <div class="metric-value" id="errorRate-\${service.id}">--%</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="metric">
                            <div class="metric-label">Requests</div>
                            <div class="metric-value" id="requests-\${service.id}">--/s</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="metric">
                            <div class="metric-label">CPU</div>
                            <div class="metric-value" id="cpu-\${service.id}">--%</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="controls">
                        <button onclick="restartService('\${service.id}')">Restart</button>
                        <button onclick="viewLogs('\${service.id}')">Logs</button>
                        <button onclick="viewMetrics('\${service.id}')">Metrics</button>
                    </div>
                \`;
                grid.appendChild(card);
            });
            
            updateServiceStatus();
        }

        async function updateServiceStatus() {
            for (const service of services) {
                const health = await checkServiceHealth(service);
                const statusEl = document.getElementById(\`status-\${service.id}\`);
                statusEl.className = \`status \${health.status}\`;
                
                // Simulate metrics for demo
                document.getElementById(\`latency-\${service.id}\`).textContent = 
                    Math.floor(Math.random() * 150 + 50) + ' ms';
                document.getElementById(\`errorRate-\${service.id}\`).textContent = 
                    (Math.random() * 2).toFixed(2) + '%';
                document.getElementById(\`requests-\${service.id}\`).textContent = 
                    Math.floor(Math.random() * 500 + 100) + '/s';
                document.getElementById(\`cpu-\${service.id}\`).textContent = 
                    Math.floor(Math.random() * 30 + 10) + '%';
            }
        }

        function refreshAll() {
            updateServiceStatus();
            showAlert('Refreshed all service statuses', 'info');
        }

        async function runHealthChecks() {
            showAlert('Running comprehensive health checks...', 'info');
            await updateServiceStatus();
            showAlert('Health checks completed', 'success');
        }

        function showPerformanceMetrics() {
            showAlert('Opening performance dashboard...', 'info');
            // In real implementation, this would open a Grafana dashboard
        }

        function restartService(serviceId) {
            showAlert(\`Restarting \${serviceId}...\`, 'warning');
            // In real implementation, this would call Kubernetes

```typescript
// src/App.tsx - Ponto de entrada principal
import React, { Suspense, lazy } from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { PremiumProvider } from './contexts/PremiumContext';
import { ErrorBoundary } from './components/ErrorBoundary';
import { LoadingSpinner } from './components/LoadingSpinner';
import { Layout } from './components/Layout';
import './styles/global.css';

// Lazy loading de rotas premium
const Dashboard = lazy(() => import('./pages/Dashboard').then(module => ({ 
  default: module.Dashboard 
})));

const Analytics = lazy(() => import('./pages/Analytics').then(module => ({ 
  default: module.Analytics 
})));

const Templates = lazy(() => import('./pages/Templates').then(module => ({ 
  default: module.Templates 
})));

const Settings = lazy(() => import('./pages/Settings').then(module => ({ 
  default: module.Settings 
})));

function App() {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <PremiumProvider>
        <Router>
          <Layout>
            <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner fullScreen />}>
              <Routes>
                <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
                <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
                <Route path="/analytics" element={<Analytics />} />
                <Route path="/templates" element={<Templates />} />
                <Route path="/settings" element={<Settings />} />
                <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
              </Routes>
            </Suspense>
          </Layout>
        </Router>
      </PremiumProvider>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
}

export default App;
