```typescript
// src/contexts/PremiumContext.tsx - Estado global otimizado
import React, { createContext, useContext, useReducer, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
import { premiumApi } from '../services/api';
import type { PremiumUser, FeatureFlags, SubscriptionPlan } from '../types/premium';

interface PremiumState {
  user: PremiumUser | null;
  features: FeatureFlags;
  subscription: SubscriptionPlan | null;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
}

type PremiumAction =
  | { type: 'SET_USER'; payload: PremiumUser }
  | { type: 'SET_FEATURES'; payload: FeatureFlags }
  | { type: 'SET_SUBSCRIPTION'; payload: SubscriptionPlan }
  | { type: 'SET_LOADING'; payload: boolean }
  | { type: 'SET_ERROR'; payload: string | null }
  | { type: 'LOGOUT' };

interface PremiumContextType extends PremiumState {
  login: (email: string, password: string) => Promise<void>;
  logout: () => void;
  refreshFeatures: () => Promise<void>;
  updateSubscription: (planId: string) => Promise<void>;
}

const initialState: PremiumState = {
  user: null,
  features: {
    advancedAnalytics: false,
    customTemplates: false,
    teamCollaboration: false,
    apiAccess: false,
    prioritySupport: false,
  },
  subscription: null,
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
};

const PremiumContext = createContext<PremiumContextType | undefined>(undefined);

function premiumReducer(state: PremiumState, action: PremiumAction): PremiumState {
  switch (action.type) {
    case 'SET_USER':
      return { ...state, user: action.payload, error: null };
    case 'SET_FEATURES':
      return { ...state, features: action.payload };
    case 'SET_SUBSCRIPTION':
      return { ...state, subscription: action.payload };
    case 'SET_LOADING':
      return { ...state, isLoading: action.payload };
    case 'SET_ERROR':
      return { ...state, error: action.payload };
    case 'LOGOUT':
      return initialState;
    default:
      return state;
  }
}

export function PremiumProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(premiumReducer, initialState);

  const login = useCallback(async (email: string, password: string) => {
    dispatch({ type: 'SET_LOADING', payload: true });
    dispatch({ type: 'SET_ERROR', payload: null });

    try {
      const { user, features, subscription } = await premiumApi.login(email, password);
      dispatch({ type: 'SET_USER', payload: user });
      dispatch({ type: 'SET_FEATURES', payload: features });
      dispatch({ type: 'SET_SUBSCRIPTION', payload: subscription });
    } catch (error) {
      dispatch({ 
        type: 'SET_ERROR', 
        payload: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Login failed' 
      });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      dispatch({ type: 'SET_LOADING', payload: false });
    }
  }, []);

  const logout = useCallback(() => {
    premiumApi.logout();
    dispatch({ type: 'LOGOUT' });
  }, []);

  const refreshFeatures = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!state.user) return;
    
    try {
      const features = await premiumApi.getFeatures(state.user.id);
      dispatch({ type: 'SET_FEATURES', payload: features });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to refresh features:', error);
    }
  }, [state.user]);

  const updateSubscription = useCallback(async (planId: string) => {
    if (!state.user) return;
    
    dispatch({ type: 'SET_LOADING', payload: true });
    
    try {
      const subscription = await premiumApi.updateSubscription(state.user.id, planId);
      dispatch({ type: 'SET_SUBSCRIPTION', payload: subscription });
    } catch (error) {
      dispatch({ 
        type: 'SET_ERROR', 
        payload: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Subscription update failed' 
      });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      dispatch({ type: 'SET_LOADING', payload: false });
    }
  }, [state.user]);

  const value = useMemo(() => ({
    ...state,
    login,
    logout,
    refreshFeatures,
    updateSubscription,
  }), [state, login, logout, refreshFeatures, updateSubscription]);

  return (
    <PremiumContext.Provider value={value}>
      {children}
    </PremiumContext.Provider>
  );
}

export function usePremium() {
  const context = useContext(PremiumContext);
  if (context === undefined) {
    throw new Error('usePremium must be used within a PremiumProvider');
  }
  return context;
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/VirtualizedList.tsx - Virtualização de listas
import React, { useRef, useCallback, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useResizeObserver } from '../hooks/useResizeObserver';
import './VirtualizedList.css';

interface VirtualizedListProps<T> {
  items: T[];
  itemHeight: number;
  renderItem: (item: T, index: number) => React.ReactNode;
  overscan?: number;
  className?: string;
}

export function VirtualizedList<T>({
  items,
  itemHeight,
  renderItem,
  overscan = 3,
  className = '',
}: VirtualizedListProps<T>) {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [scrollTop, setScrollTop] = useState(0);
  const [containerHeight, setContainerHeight] = useState(0);
  
  const { width } = useResizeObserver(containerRef);

  const handleScroll = useCallback((event: React.UIEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    setScrollTop(event.currentTarget.scrollTop);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (containerRef.current) {
      setContainerHeight(containerRef.current.clientHeight);
    }
  }, [width]);

  const totalHeight = items.length * itemHeight;
  const startIndex = Math.max(0, Math.floor(scrollTop / itemHeight) - overscan);
  const endIndex = Math.min(
    items.length - 1,
    Math.floor((scrollTop + containerHeight) / itemHeight) + overscan
  );

  const visibleItems = items.slice(startIndex, endIndex + 1);
  const offsetY = startIndex * itemHeight;

  return (
    <div
      ref={containerRef}
      className={`virtualized-list ${className}`}
      onScroll={handleScroll}
      style={{ overflowY: 'auto', position: 'relative' }}
    >
      <div style={{ height: totalHeight, position: 'relative' }}>
        <div
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            top: offsetY,
            width: '100%',
          }}
        >
          {visibleItems.map((item, index) => (
            <div
              key={startIndex + index}
              style={{ height: itemHeight }}
            >
              {renderItem(item, startIndex + index)}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

// src/pages/Dashboard.tsx - Página principal com lazy loading de componentes
import React, { Suspense, lazy, useMemo } from 'react';
import { usePremium } from '../contexts/PremiumContext';

// Lazy loading de componentes pesados do dashboard
const ActivityChart = lazy(() => 
  import('../components/charts/ActivityChart').then(module => ({
    default: module.ActivityChart
  }))
);

const RecentProjects = lazy(() => 
  import('../components/RecentProjects').then(module => ({
    default: module.RecentProjects
  }))
);

const TeamCollaboration = lazy(() => 
  import('../components/TeamCollaboration').then(module => ({
    default: module.TeamCollaboration
  }))
);

export function Dashboard() {
  const { user, features, isLoading } = usePremium();
  
  const stats = useMemo(() => [
    { label: 'Active Projects', value: '12', change: '+2', trend: 'up' },
    { label: 'Team Members', value: '8', change: '+1', trend: 'up' },
    { label: 'Storage Used', value: '4.2 GB', change: '-0.3', trend: 'down' },
    { label: 'API Calls', value: '1.2K', change: '+120', trend: 'up' },
  ], []);

  if (isLoading) {
    return <LoadingSpinner fullScreen />;
  }

  return (
    <div className="dashboard">
      <header className="dashboard-header">
        <h1>Welcome back, {user?.name || 'User'}</h1>
        <p className="dashboard-subtitle">
          {features.prioritySupport ? '✨ Priority Support Active' : 'Standard Account'}
        </p>
      </header>

      <StatsGrid stats={stats} />
      
      <QuickActions />

      <div className="dashboard-grid">
        <div className="dashboard-column">
          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
            <ActivityChart />
          </Suspense>
        </div>
        
        <div className="dashboard-column">
          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
            <RecentProjects />
          </Suspense>
        </div>
      </div>

      {features.teamCollaboration && (
        <div className="dashboard-section">
          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
            <TeamCollaboration />
          </Suspense>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

```typescript
// src/hooks/useImageLoader.ts - Hook para lazy loading de imagens otimizado
import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

interface UseImageLoaderOptions {
  src: string;
  placeholder?: string;
  fallback?: string;
  threshold?: number;
  rootMargin?: string;
}

export function useImageLoader({
  src,
  placeholder = 'data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMTAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjEwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDEwMCAxMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+PHJlY3Qgd2lkdGg9IjEwMCIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxMDAiIGZpbGw9IiNGMEYwRjAiLz48L3N2Zz4=',
  fallback = 'data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMTAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjEwMCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDEwMCAxMDAiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+PHJlY3Qgd2lkdGg9IjEwMCIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxMDAiIGZpbGw9IiNGRjAwMDAiLz48dGV4dCB4PSI1MCIgeT0iNTAiIGZvbnQtZmFtaWx5PSJBcmlhbCIgZm9udC1zaXplPSIxMiIgZmlsbD0id2hpdGUiIHRleHQtYW5jaG9yPSJtaWRkbGUiIGR5PSIuM2VtIj5FcnJvcjwvdGV4dD48L3N2Zz4=',
  threshold = 0.1,
  rootMargin = '50px',
}: UseImageLoaderOptions) {
  const [imageSrc, setImageSrc] = useState(placeholder);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [hasError, setHasError] = useState(false);
  const imgRef = useRef<HTMLImageElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!src) {
      setImageSrc(fallback);
      setIsLoading(false);
      return;
    }

    setIsLoading(true);
    setHasError(false);
    setImageSrc(placeholder);

    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      (entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            const img = new Image();
            
            img.src = src;
            img.onload = () => {
              setImageSrc(src);
              setIsLoading(false);
            };
            
            img.onerror = () => {
              setImageSrc(fallback);
              setIsLoading(false);
              setHasError(true);
            };

            observer.disconnect();
          }
        });
      },
      { threshold, rootMargin }
    );

    if (imgRef.current) {
      observer.observe(imgRef.current);
    }

    return () => {
      observer.disconnect();
    };
  }, [src, placeholder, fallback, threshold, rootMargin]);

  return { imageSrc, isLoading, hasError, imgRef };
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/ImageLazy.tsx - Componente de imagem com lazy loading
import React from 'react';
import { useImageLoader } from '../hooks/useImageLoader';
import './ImageLazy.css';

interface ImageLazyProps extends React.ImgHTMLAttributes<HTMLImageElement> {
  src: string;
  alt: string;
  placeholder?: string;
  fallback?: string;
  threshold?: number;
  rootMargin?: string;
}

export function ImageLazy({
  src,
  alt,
  placeholder,
  fallback,
  threshold = 0.1,
  rootMargin = '50px',
  className = '',
  ...props
}: ImageLazyProps) {
  const { imageSrc, isLoading, hasError, imgRef } = useImageLoader({
    src,
    placeholder,
    fallback,
    threshold,
    rootMargin,
  });

  return (
    <img
      ref={imgRef}
      src={imageSrc}
      alt={alt}
      className={`image-lazy ${isLoading ? 'image-lazy--loading' : ''} ${
        hasError ? 'image-lazy--error' : ''
      } ${className}`}
      loading="lazy"
      decoding="async"
      {...props}
    />
  );
}
```

```typescript
// src/services/api.ts - Serviço de API com tratamento de erros e retry
import axios, { AxiosInstance, AxiosError } from 'axios';

const API_BASE_URL = process.env.REACT_APP_API_URL || 'https://api.diyapp.com/v1';

interface ApiConfig {
  baseURL: string;
  timeout: number;
  headers: Record<string, string>;
}

interface RetryConfig {
  maxRetries: number;
  baseDelay: number;
  maxDelay: number;
}

class PremiumApiService {
  private client: AxiosInstance;
  private retryConfig: RetryConfig;

  constructor() {
    const config: ApiConfig = {
      baseURL: API_BASE_URL,
      timeout: 10000,
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Accept': 'application/json',
      },
    };

    this.client = axios.create(config);
    this.retryConfig = {
      maxRetries: 3,
      baseDelay: 1000,
      maxDelay: 10000,
    };

    this.setupInterceptors();
  }

  private setupInterceptors() {
    // Request interceptor para adicionar token
    this.client.interceptors.request.use(
      (config) => {
        const token = localStorage.getItem('premium_token');
        if (token) {
          config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
        }
        return config;
      },
      (error) => Promise.reject(error)
    );

    // Response interceptor para tratamento de erros
    this.client.interceptors.response.use(
      (response) => response,
      async (error: AxiosError) => {
        const originalRequest = error.config;
        
        if (!originalRequest) {
          return Promise.reject(error);
        }

        // Retry para erros de rede ou 5xx
        if (this.shouldRetry(error)) {
          return this.retryRequest(originalRequest, error);
        }

       

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```javascript
// DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core
// Refatoração de APIs para GraphQL/REST híbrido com cache Redis, filas assíncronas e PostgreSQL otimizado

// Estrutura do projeto:
// src/
//   ├── server.js              # Ponto de entrada principal
//   ├── config/               # Configurações
//   ├── graphql/              # Schema e resolvers GraphQL
//   ├── rest/                 # APIs REST tradicionais
//   ├── services/             # Lógica de negócio
//   ├── repositories/         # Acesso a dados
//   ├── queues/               # Jobs assíncronos (Bull)
//   ├── cache/                # Redis client e helpers
//   ├── database/             # PostgreSQL connection pool
//   └── middleware/           # Middlewares compartilhados

// ==================== server.js ====================
const express = require('express');
const { ApolloServer } = require('apollo-server-express');
const { createServer } = require('http');
const { execute, subscribe } = require('graphql');
const { SubscriptionServer } = require('subscriptions-transport-ws');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const compression = require('compression');

// Configurações
const config = require('./config');
const { logger, requestLogger } = require('./middleware/logger');
const { errorHandler } = require('./middleware/errorHandler');
const { authenticate, authorize } = require('./middleware/auth');
const { redisClient } = require('./cache/redis');
const { pgPool } = require('./database/postgres');
const { bullQueue } = require('./queues');

class DIYAppServer {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.httpServer = createServer(this.app);
    this.apolloServer = null;
    this.isShuttingDown = false;
    
    this.setupProcessHandlers();
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupHealthChecks();
    this.setupRoutes();
  }

  setupProcessHandlers() {
    // Graceful shutdown
    const gracefulShutdown = async (signal) => {
      if (this.isShuttingDown) return;
      
      this.isShuttingDown = true;
      logger.info(`Received ${signal}, starting graceful shutdown...`);
      
      try {
        // Parar novas requisições
        this.httpServer.close(async () => {
          logger.info('HTTP server closed');
          
          // Fechar Apollo Server
          if (this.apolloServer) {
            await this.apolloServer.stop();
            logger.info('Apollo Server stopped');
          }
          
          // Fechar conexões
          await Promise.allSettled([
            redisClient.quit().catch(err => logger.error('Redis close error:', err)),
            pgPool.end().catch(err => logger.error('PostgreSQL close error:', err)),
            bullQueue.close().catch(err => logger.error('Bull queue close error:', err))
          ]);
          
          logger.info('Graceful shutdown completed');
          process.exit(0);
        });
        
        // Timeout de 30 segundos
        setTimeout(() => {
          logger.error('Graceful shutdown timeout, forcing exit');
          process.exit(1);
        }, 30000);
        
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Shutdown error:', error);
        process.exit(1);
      }
    };

    process.on('SIGTERM', () => gracefulShutdown('SIGTERM'));
    process.on('SIGINT', () => gracefulShutdown('SIGINT'));
    
    // Unhandled rejections
    process.on('unhandledRejection', (reason, promise) => {
      logger.error('Unhandled Rejection at:', promise, 'reason:', reason);
      // Não sair em produção, apenas logar
    });
  }

  setupMiddleware() {
    // Security
    this.app.use(helmet({
      contentSecurityPolicy: config.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? undefined : false
    }));
    
    // CORS
    this.app.use(cors({
      origin: config.CORS_ORIGINS,
      credentials: true,
      optionsSuccessStatus: 200
    }));
    
    // Rate limiting para APIs públicas
    const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
      max: 100, // limite por IP
      message: 'Too many requests from this IP',
      standardHeaders: true,
      legacyHeaders: false,
      skip: (req) => req.path.includes('/health') || req.ip === '127.0.0.1'
    });
    
    this.app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);
    
    // Compression
    this.app.use(compression());
    
    // Body parsing
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));
    
    // Request logging
    this.app.use(requestLogger);
    
    // Correlation ID
    this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
      req.correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || 
                         req.headers['x-request-id'] || 
                         `corr-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
      res.setHeader('X-Correlation-ID', req.correlationId);
      next();
    });
  }

  setupHealthChecks() {
    // Health check simples
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.status(200).json({ 
        status: 'healthy',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        uptime: process.uptime()
      });
    });
    
    // Health check detalhado
    this.app.get('/health/detailed', async (req, res) => {
      const checks = {
        redis: 'pending',
        postgresql: 'pending',
        bull: 'pending'
      };
      
      try {
        // Redis
        await redisClient.ping();
        checks.redis = 'healthy';
      } catch (error) {
        checks.redis = 'unhealthy';
        logger.error('Redis health check failed:', error);
      }
      
      try {
        // PostgreSQL
        const client = await pgPool.connect();
        await client.query('SELECT 1');
        client.release();
        checks.postgresql = 'healthy';
      } catch (error) {
        checks.postgresql = 'unhealthy';
        logger.error('PostgreSQL health check failed:', error);
      }
      
      try {
        // Bull queue
        await bullQueue.getJobCounts();
        checks.bull = 'healthy';
      } catch (error) {
        checks.bull = 'unhealthy';
        logger.error('Bull health check failed:', error);
      }
      
      const allHealthy = Object.values(checks).every(status => status === 'healthy');
      
      res.status(allHealthy ? 200 : 503).json({
        status: allHealthy ? 'healthy' : 'degraded',
        checks,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    });
  }

  async setupApolloServer() {
    const { typeDefs, resolvers } = require('./graphql');
    const { makeExecutableSchema } = require('@graphql-tools/schema');
    
    const schema = makeExecutableSchema({
      typeDefs,
      resolvers
    });
    
    this.apolloServer = new ApolloServer({
      schema,
      context: ({ req }) => ({
        req,
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        userId: req.user?.id,
        redis: redisClient,
        pgPool,
        bullQueue
      }),
      plugins: [{
        async requestDidStart(requestContext) {
          const startTime = Date.now();
          const { request, context } = requestContext;
          
          return {
            async willSendResponse(responseContext) {
              const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
              const operationName = request.operationName || 'anonymous';
              
              logger.info({
                level: 'info',
                correlation_id: context.correlationId,
                user_id: context.userId,
                operation: operationName,
                duration_ms: duration,
                query_complexity: request.query?.length || 0
              });
              
              // Alertar se query muito lenta
              if (duration > 1000) {
                logger.warn({
                  level: 'warn',
                  message: 'Slow GraphQL query',
                  correlation_id: context.correlationId,
                  operation: operationName,
                  duration_ms: duration
                });
              }
            },
            async didEncounterErrors(requestContext) {
              const { errors, context } = requestContext;
              
              errors.forEach(error => {
                logger.error({
                  level: 'error',
                  correlation_id: context.correlationId,
                  user_id: context.userId,
                  error: error.message,
                  path: error.path,
                  stack: config.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.stack : undefined
                });
              });
            }
          };
        }
      }],
      formatError: (error) => {
        // Nunca expor stack trace em produção
        const formattedError = {
          message: error.message,
          locations: error.locations,
          path: error.path
        };
        
        if (config.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
          formattedError.extensions = error.extensions;
        }
        
        return formattedError;
      }
    });
    
    await this.apolloServer.start();
    this.apolloServer.applyMiddleware({ 
      app: this.app,
      path: '/graphql',
      cors: false
    });
    
    // WebSocket para subscriptions
    SubscriptionServer.create(
      {
        schema,
        execute,
        subscribe,
        onConnect: (connectionParams, webSocket) => {
          // Implementar autenticação WebSocket aqui
          return { webSocket };
        }
      },
      {
        server: this.httpServer,
        path: '/graphql'
      }
    );
  }

  setupRoutes() {
    // APIs REST
    const restRouter = require('./rest');
    this.app.use('/api/v1', authenticate, restRouter);
    
    // Error handler deve ser o último middleware
    this.app.use(errorHandler);
  }

  async start() {
    try {
      // Inicializar conexões
      await Promise.all([
        redisClient.connect().then(() => logger.info('Redis connected')),
        pgPool.connect().then(() => logger.info('PostgreSQL connected')),
        bullQueue.isReady().then(() => logger.info('Bull queue ready'))
      ]);
      
      // Configurar Apollo Server
      await this.setupApolloServer();
      
      // Iniciar servidor
      const PORT = config.PORT || 3000;
      this.httpServer.listen(PORT, () => {
        logger.info(`Server running on port ${PORT}`);
        logger.info(`GraphQL endpoint: http://localhost:${PORT}/graphql`);
        logger.info(`REST API endpoint: http://localhost:${PORT}/api/v1`);
      });
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to start server:', error);
      process.exit(1);
    }
  }
}

// Iniciar servidor se executado diretamente
if (require.main === module) {
  const server = new DIYAppServer();
  server.start();
}

module.exports = DIYAppServer;
```

```javascript
// ==================== database/postgres.js ====================
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const config = require('../config');
const logger = require('../middleware/logger');

class PostgreSQLConnection {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = new Pool({
      host: config.PG_HOST,
      port: config.PG_PORT,
      database: config.PG_DATABASE,
      user: config.PG_USER,
      password: config.PG_PASSWORD,
      max: config.PG_MAX_CONNECTIONS,
      idleTimeoutMillis: config.PG_IDLE_TIMEOUT,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: config.DB_QUERY_TIMEOUT,
      
      // Configurações de performance
      application_name: 'diyapp-v11',
      statement_timeout: config.DB_QUERY_TIMEOUT,
      
      // SSL se necessário
      ssl: config.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? {
        rejectUnauthorized: false
      } : false
    });
    
    this.setupEventListeners();
    this.setupConnectionTesting();
  }
  
  setupEventListeners() {
    this.pool.on('connect', (client) => {
      logger.debug('New PostgreSQL client connected');
    });
    
    this.pool.on('error', (err, client) => {
      logger.error('Unexpected PostgreSQL pool error:', err);
      // Não lançar erro aqui para evitar crash
    });
    
    this.pool.on('remove', (client) => {
      logger.debug('PostgreSQL client removed from pool');
    });
  }
  
  setupConnectionTesting() {
    // Testar conexão periodicamente
    setInterval(async () => {
      try {
        const client = await this.pool.connect();
        await client.query('SELECT 1');
        client.release();
        logger.debug('PostgreSQL connection test passed');
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('PostgreSQL connection test failed:', error);
      }
    }, 300000); // A cada 5 minutos
  }
  
  async query(text, params = [], options = {}) {
    const startTime = Date.now();
    const correlationId = options.correlationId || 'unknown';
    
    try {
      // SEMPRE usar parâmetros preparados
      const result = await this.pool.query({
        text,
        values: params,
        rowMode: 'array',
        ...options
      });
      
      const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
      
      // Log de queries lentas
      if (duration > 1000) {
        logger.warn({
          level: 'warn',
          message: 'Slow PostgreSQL query',
          correlation_id: correlationId,
          query: text.substring(0, 200), // Log apenas parte da query
          params: this.maskSensitiveData(params),
          duration_ms: duration,
          row_count: result.rowCount
        });
      }
      
      return result;
      
    } catch (error) {
      const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
      
      logger.error({
        level: 'error',
        message: 'PostgreSQL query error',
        correlation_id: correlationId,
        query: text.substring(0, 200),
        params: this.maskSensitiveData(params),
        duration_ms: duration,
        error: error.message,
        code: error.code
      });
      
      // Classificar erros
      if (error.code === '23505') { // Unique violation
        const customError = new Error('Duplicate entry');
        customError.code = 'CONFLICT';
        customError.statusCode = 409;
        throw customError;
      }
      
      if (error.code === '23503') { // Foreign key violation
        const customError = new Error('Referenced resource not found');
        customError.code = 'NOT_FOUND';
        customError.statusCode = 404;
        throw customError;
      }
      
      // Timeout
      if (error.code === '57014') {
        const customError = new Error('Query timeout');
        customError.code = 'TIMEOUT';
        customError.statusCode = 504;
        throw customError;
      }
      
      // Re-lançar erro genérico
      const dbError = new Error('Database error');
      dbError.originalError = error;
      dbError.statusCode = 500;
      throw dbError;
    }
  }
  
  async transaction(callback, options = {}) {
    const client = await this.pool

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Telemetria Analítica

## Arquitetura do Sistema de Telemetria

```
DIYAPP Telemetry Analytics
├── Real-time Pipeline (Kafka/WebSockets)
├── Batch Processing (dbt)
├── Analytics Dashboard (Streamlit/Plotly)
└── Monitoring & Alerts
```

## 1. Esquema Analítico de Telemetria (BigQuery/SQL)

-- schema/telemetry_schema.sql
-- Camada RAW (bronze) - Dados brutos preservados
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp_analytics.raw_telemetry_events`
(
  event_id STRING NOT NULL,
  session_id STRING NOT NULL,
  user_id STRING,
  device_id STRING NOT NULL,
  event_type STRING NOT NULL,  -- 'page_view', 'feature_click', 'api_call', 'error', 'conversion'
  event_name STRING NOT NULL,  -- nome específico do evento
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
  received_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
  platform STRING,  -- 'web', 'mobile_ios', 'mobile_android', 'desktop'
  app_version STRING,
  os_version STRING,
  browser STRING,
  country_code STRING,
  city STRING,
  screen_resolution STRING,
  language STRING,
  utm_source STRING,
  utm_medium STRING,
  utm_campaign STRING,
  page_url STRING,
  page_title STRING,
  referrer_url STRING,
  event_duration_ms INT64,
  event_properties JSON,  -- propriedades específicas do evento
  error_details JSON,     -- detalhes de erro se aplicável
  metadata JSON          -- metadados adicionais
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY event_type, platform, country_code
OPTIONS(
  description='Tabela RAW de eventos de telemetria - nunca deletar',
  require_partition_filter=true
);

(

  error_5xx_count INT64 NOT NULL,
  -- Métricas de SLA
  sla_violations INT64 NOT NULL,  -- respostas > 500ms
  sla_compliance_rate FLOAT64 NOT NULL,
  -- Métricas de Business
  success_rate FLOAT64 NOT NULL,
  timeout_count INT64,
  -- Metadados
  data_quality_score FLOAT64 NOT NULL,
  processing_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(metric_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY api_endpoint, metric_interval
OPTIONS(
  description='Performance de API em tempo quase real - latência < 5min',
  require_partition_filter=true
);

## 2. Pipeline de Tempo Real (Kafka + WebSockets)

```python
# src/real_time_pipeline/kafka_consumer.py
import json
import asyncio
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from enum import Enum

import aiokafka
import websockets
from google.cloud import bigquery
from google.api_core.exceptions import GoogleAPIError
import uvloop

# Configurar logging profissional
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('logs/telemetry_pipeline.log'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# Configurações
class Config:
    KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS = "localhost:9092"
    KAFKA_TOPIC_TELEMETRY = "diyapp-telemetry-events"
    KAFKA_CONSUMER_GROUP = "telemetry-processor-v1"
    KAFKA_AUTO_OFFSET_RESET = "latest"
    
    WEBSOCKET_HOST = "0.0.0.0"
    WEBSOCKET_PORT = 8765
    WEBSOCKET_PATH = "/realtime/metrics"
    
    BIGQUERY_PROJECT = "diyapp-analytics"
    BIGQUERY_DATASET = "diyapp_analytics"
    BIGQUERY_TABLE_RAW = "raw_telemetry_events"
    
    BATCH_SIZE = 100
    BATCH_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 5
    
    # Quality thresholds
    MAX_EVENT_AGE_SECONDS = 3600  # 1 hora
    MIN_EVENT_TIMESTAMP = "2024-01-01"

@dataclass
class TelemetryEvent:
    """Schema validado para eventos de telemetria"""
    event_id: str
    session_id: str
    user_id: Optional[str]
    device_id: str
    event_type: str
    event_name: str
    event_timestamp: str  # ISO format
    received_at: str      # ISO format
    platform: Optional[str]
    app_version: Optional[str]
    os_version: Optional[str]
    browser: Optional[str]
    country_code: Optional[str]
    city: Optional[str]
    screen_resolution: Optional[str]
    language: Optional[str]
    utm_source: Optional[str]
    utm_medium: Optional[str]
    utm_campaign: Optional[str]
    page_url: Optional[str]
    page_title: Optional[str]
    referrer_url: Optional[str]
    event_duration_ms: Optional[int]
    event_properties: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]
    error_details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]
    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]
    
    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional['TelemetryEvent']:
        """Valida e cria evento a partir de dict"""
        try:
            # Validações básicas
            required_fields = ['event_id', 'session_id', 'device_id', 
                             'event_type', 'event_name', 'event_timestamp']
            
            for field in required_fields:
                if field not in data or not data[field]:
                    logger.warning(f"Campo obrigatório faltando: {field}")
                    return None
            
            # Valida timestamp
            try:
                event_dt = datetime.fromisoformat(data['event_timestamp'].replace('Z', '+00:00'))
                received_dt = datetime.fromisoformat(
                    data.get('received_at', datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()).replace('Z', '+00:00')
                )
                
                # Verifica se evento não é muito antigo
                age_seconds = (received_dt - event_dt).total_seconds()
                if age_seconds > Config.MAX_EVENT_AGE_SECONDS:
                    logger.warning(f"Evento muito antigo: {age_seconds} segundos")
                    return None
                    
            except ValueError:
                logger.warning(f"Timestamp inválido: {data.get('event_timestamp')}")
                return None
            
            return cls(**data)
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao validar evento: {e}")
            return None

class EventProcessor:
    """Processador de eventos em tempo real"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.bigquery_client = bigquery.Client()
        self.event_buffer = []
        self.last_flush_time = datetime.now()
        self.metrics_aggregator = MetricsAggregator()
        self.quality_checker = DataQualityChecker()
        
    async def process_event(self, event_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """Processa um único evento"""
        try:
            # Valida evento
            event = TelemetryEvent.from_dict(event_data)
            if not event:
                logger.warning("Evento inválido descartado")
                return False
            
            # Verifica qualidade
            quality_score = self.quality_checker.check_event_quality(event)
            if quality_score < 0.7:
                logger.warning(f"Evento com baixa qualidade: {quality_score}")
                # Ainda processamos, mas marcamos como baixa qualidade
            
            # Adiciona metadados de qualidade
            event_dict = asdict(event)
            event_dict['data_quality_score'] = quality_score
            event_dict['processing_timestamp'] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
            
            # Buffer para batch insert
            self.event_buffer.append(event_dict)
            
            # Atualiza agregadores em tempo real
            await self.metrics_aggregator.update(event_dict)
            
            # Verifica se deve fazer flush
            if (len(self.event_buffer) >= Config.BATCH_SIZE or 
                (datetime.now() - self.last_flush_time).seconds >= Config.BATCH_TIMEOUT_SECONDS):
                await self.flush_buffer()
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao processar evento: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def flush_buffer(self):
        """Envia batch para BigQuery"""
        if not self.event_buffer:
            return
            
        try:
            table_ref = f"{Config.BIGQUERY_PROJECT}.{Config.BIGQUERY_DATASET}.{Config.BIGQUERY_TABLE_RAW}"
            errors = self.bigquery_client.insert_rows_json(
                table_ref, 
                self.event_buffer
            )
            
            if errors:
                logger.error(f"Erros ao inserir no BigQuery: {errors}")
                # TODO: Implementar dead letter queue
            else:
                logger.info(f"Batch de {len(self.event_buffer)} eventos inserido com sucesso")
                
            # Limpa buffer
            self.event_buffer.clear()
            self.last_flush_time = datetime.now()
            
        except GoogleAPIError as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro de API do Google: {e}")
            # TODO: Implementar retry com backoff exponencial
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro inesperado ao fazer flush: {e}")

class MetricsAggregator:
    """Agrega métricas em tempo real para WebSockets"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.realtime_metrics = {
            'active_sessions': set(),
            'events_per_minute': [],
            'error_count': 0,
            'conversion_count': 0,
            'api_response_times': [],
            'feature_usage': {}
        }
        self.websocket_clients = set()
        
    async def update(self, event: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Atualiza métricas em tempo real"""
        current_time = datetime.now()
        
        # Atualiza sessões ativas
        self.realtime_metrics['active_sessions'].add(event['session_id'])
        
        # Limpa sessões antigas (últimos 30 minutos)
        # Nota: Em produção, usaríamos timestamp do evento
        
        # Conta eventos por minuto
        self.realtime_metrics['events_per_minute'].append(current_time)
        
        # Limpa eventos antigos (mantém apenas últimos 5 minutos)
        five_min_ago = current_time.timestamp() - 300
        self.realtime_metrics['events_per_minute'] = [
            ts for ts in self.realtime_metrics['events_per_minute']
            if ts.timestamp() > five_min_ago
        ]
        
        # Conta erros e conversões
        if event['event_type'] == 'error':
            self.realtime_metrics['error_count'] += 1
        elif event['event_type'] == 'conversion':
            self.realtime_metrics['conversion_count'] += 1
            
        # Coleta tempos de resposta de API
        if event['event_type'] == 'api_call' and event.get('event_properties', {}).get('response_time'):
            self.realtime_metrics['api_response_times'].append(
                event['event_properties']['response_time']
            )
            # Mantém apenas últimos 1000 valores
            if len(self.realtime_metrics['api_response_times']) > 1000:
                self.realtime_metrics['api_response_times'] = self.realtime_metrics['api_response_times'][-1000:]
        
        # Rastreia uso de features
        if event['event_type'] == 'feature_click':
            feature_name = event.get('event_properties', {}).get('feature_name', 'unknown')
            self.realtime_metrics['feature_usage'][feature_name] = \
                self.realtime_metrics['

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]

## 1. Terraform - Infraestrutura como Código

### `terraform/providers.tf`
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }
  
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "v11/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
    token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
  }
}
```

### `terraform/variables.tf`

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name (dev, staging, prod)"
  type        = string
  default     = "prod"
  
  validation {
    condition     = contains(["dev", "staging", "prod"], var.environment)
    error_message = "Environment must be dev, staging, or prod."
  }
}

variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "EKS cluster name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp-v11-cluster"
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "VPC CIDR block"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "Availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b", "us-east-1c"]
}

variable "node_instance_types" {
  description = "EKS node instance types"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["t3.medium", "t3.large"]
}

variable "min_nodes" {
  description = "Minimum number of nodes"
  type        = number
  default     = 3
}

variable "max_nodes" {
  description = "Maximum number of nodes"
  type        = number
  default     = 10
}

variable "desired_nodes" {
  description = "Desired number of nodes"
  type        = number
  default     = 3
}

variable "slo_availability" {
  description = "SLO Availability target"
  type        = number
  default     = 99.9
}

  description = "SLO Latency P95 target in ms"
  type        = number
  default     = 300

  name = module.eks.cluster_name

# VPC Module

  source = "./modules/vpc"
  
  name                 = "diyapp-v11-${var.environment}"
  cidr                 = var.vpc_cidr
  azs                  = var.availability_zones
  private_subnets      = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
  public_subnets       = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]
  enable_nat_gateway   = true
  single_nat_gateway   = false
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
  }
}

# EKS Module
module "eks" {
  source = "./modules/eks"
  
  cluster_name    = "${var.cluster_name}-${var.environment}"
  cluster_version = "1.28"
  vpc_id          = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids      = module.vpc.private_subnets
  
  node_groups = {
    main = {
      min_size     = var.min_nodes
      max_size     = var.max_nodes
      desired_size = var.desired_nodes
      
      instance_types = var.node_instance_types
      capacity_type  = "SPOT"
      
      labels = {
        node-type = "main"
        squad     = "sre"
      }
      
      taints = []
      
      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"             = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/${var.cluster_name}" = "owned"
      }
    }
    
    monitoring = {
      min_size     = 1
      max_size     = 3
      desired_size = 1
      
      instance_types = ["t3.large"]
      capacity_type  = "ON_DEMAND"
      
      labels = {
        node-type = "monitoring"
        squad     = "sre"
      }
      
      taints = [{
        key    = "monitoring"
        value  = "true"
        effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
      }]
    }
  }
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
  }
}

# RDS Module for PostgreSQL
module "rds" {
  source = "./modules/rds"
  
  environment          = var.environment
  vpc_id              = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids          = module.vpc.private_subnets
  security_group_ids  = [module.eks.cluster_primary_security_group_id]
  
  instance_class      = var.environment == "prod" ? "db.t3.large" : "db.t3.medium"
  allocated_storage   = var.environment == "prod" ? 100 : 20
  max_allocated_storage = var.environment == "prod" ? 500 : 100
  
  database_name       = "diyapp_v11"
  username           = "diyapp_admin"
  
  backup_retention_period = var.environment == "prod" ? 30 : 7
  backup_window          = "03:00-04:00"
  maintenance_window     = "sun:04:00-sun:05:00"
  
  monitoring_interval    = 60
  performance_insights_enabled = true
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
  }
}

# S3 Bucket for Terraform state

    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
  }

    status = "Enabled"
  }
}

resource "aws_s3_bucket_server_side_encryption_configuration" "terraform_state" {

  rule {
    apply_server_side_encryption_by_default {
      sse_algorithm = "AES256"
    }
  }
}

resource "aws_s3_bucket_public_access_block" "terraform_state" {
  bucket = aws_s3_bucket.terraform_state.id
  
  block_public_acls       = true
  block_public_policy     = true
  ignore_public_acls      = true
  restrict_public_buckets = true
}

# DynamoDB for Terraform state locking

  billing_mode = "PAY_PER_REQUEST"

    name = "LockID"

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
  }

# IAM Policy for Cluster Autoscaler
resource "aws_iam_policy" "cluster_autoscaler" {
  name        = "DIYAPP-ClusterAutoscaler-${var.environment}"
  description = "Policy for Kubernetes Cluster Autoscaler"
  
  policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Effect = "Allow"
        Action = [
          "autoscaling:DescribeAutoScalingGroups",
          "autoscaling:DescribeAutoScalingInstances",
          "autoscaling:DescribeLaunchConfigurations",
          "autoscaling:DescribeTags",
          "autoscaling:SetDesiredCapacity",
          "autoscaling:TerminateInstanceInAutoScalingGroup",
          "ec2:DescribeLaunchTemplateVersions"
        ]
        Resource = "*"
      }
    ]
  })
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
  }
}

# Attach policy to node IAM role
resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "cluster_autoscaler" {
  policy_arn = aws_iam_policy.cluster_autoscaler.arn
  role       = module.eks.node_group_role_name
}

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Auditoria de Segurança e Implementações

## 1. Análise de Segurança do Código V10 (Auditoria STRIDE)

### Vulnerabilidades Identificadas:

```javascript
// VULNERABILIDADE CRÍTICA (CVSS 9.1): Autenticação por sessão sem tokens JWT
// Local: src/middleware/auth.js
// Problema: Sessões baseadas apenas em cookies sem validação de assinatura
app.use(session({
    secret: 'secret123', // Hardcoded secret
    resave: false,
    saveUninitialized: true
}));
```

```javascript
// VULNERABILIDADE ALTA (CVSS 8.2): SQL Injection direto
// Local: src/controllers/userController.js
// Problema: Concatenção direta de strings em queries SQL
const query = `SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = '${email}' AND password = '${password}'`;
```

```javascript
// VULNERABILIDADE ALTA (CVSS 7.5): XSS em renderização de templates
// Local: src/views/dashboard.ejs
// Problema: Dados do usuário renderizados sem sanitização
<h1>Welcome, <%= user.name %></h1>
<p><%= user.bio %></p>
```

```javascript
// VULNERABILIDADE MÉDIA (CVSS 6.8): Falta de rate limiting
// Local: src/routes/auth.js
// Problema: Endpoints de login sem limitação de tentativas
app.post('/login', (req, res) => {
    // Sem rate limiting
});
```

## 2. Implementação OAuth2.0 com OpenID Connect

### Estrutura de Pastas:
```
src/
├── auth/
│   ├── oauth2.js
│   ├── strategies/
│   │   ├── googleStrategy.js
│   │   ├── githubStrategy.js
│   │   └── microsoftStrategy.js
│   └── middleware/
│       ├── jwtAuth.js
│       └── sessionAuth.js
├── config/
│   ├── security.js
│   └── oauthProviders.js
├── utils/
│   ├── encryption.js
│   ├── sanitization.js
│   └── rateLimiter.js
└── index.js
```

### 2.1 Configuração de Segurança (src/config/security.js)

```javascript
// src/config/security.js
const crypto = require('crypto');

module.exports = {
    // Geração segura de secrets
    generateSecrets: () => {
        return {
            jwtSecret: crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex'),
            sessionSecret: crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex'),
            encryptionKey: crypto.randomBytes(32) // AES-256
        };
    },

    // Configurações de segurança
    securityConfig: {
        // JWT Configuration
        jwt: {
            algorithm: 'HS256',
            accessTokenExpiry: '15m',
            refreshTokenExpiry: '7d',
            issuer: 'diyapp-v11',
            audience: 'diyapp-users'
        },

        // Criptografia
        encryption: {
            algorithm: 'aes-256-gcm',
            ivLength: 16,
            saltLength: 32,
            iterations: 100000
        },

        // Rate Limiting
        rateLimits: {
            auth: {
                windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
                max: 5, // 5 tentativas por IP
                message: 'Too many login attempts, please try again later'
            },
            api: {
                windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minuto
                max: 100 // 100 requests por IP
            }
        },

        // Headers de Segurança
        securityHeaders: {
            contentSecurityPolicy: {
                defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
                scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
                styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
                imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
                connectSrc: ["'self'", "https://accounts.google.com", "https://github.com"],
                fontSrc: ["'self'"],
                objectSrc: ["'none'"],
                mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
                frameSrc: ["'self'"]
            },
            hsts: {
                maxAge: 31536000,
                includeSubDomains: true,
                preload: true
            }
        }
    }
};
```

### 2.2 Implementação OAuth2.0 (src/auth/oauth2.js)

```javascript
// src/auth/oauth2.js
const passport = require('passport');
const OAuth2Strategy = require('passport-oauth2').Strategy;
const JwtStrategy = require('passport-jwt').Strategy;
const { ExtractJwt } = require('passport-jwt');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const { securityConfig } = require('../config/security');

class OAuth2Manager {
    constructor() {
        this.providers = new Map();
        this.initializePassport();
    }

    initializePassport() {
        // Serialização de usuário
        passport.serializeUser((user, done) => {
            done(null, user.id);
        });

        passport.deserializeUser(async (id, done) => {
            try {
                const user = await this.findUserById(id);
                done(null, user);
            } catch (error) {
                done(error);
            }
        });

        // Estratégia JWT para API
        const jwtOptions = {
            jwtFromRequest: ExtractJwt.fromExtractors([
                ExtractJwt.fromAuthHeaderAsBearerToken(),
                ExtractJwt.fromUrlQueryParameter('token'),
                ExtractJwt.fromBodyField('token')
            ]),
            secretOrKey: process.env.JWT_SECRET || securityConfig.generateSecrets().jwtSecret,
            issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
            audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
        };

        passport.use(new JwtStrategy(jwtOptions, async (payload, done) => {
            try {
                const user = await this.validateJwtPayload(payload);
                if (user) {
                    return done(null, user);
                }
                return done(null, false);
            } catch (error) {
                return done(error, false);
            }
        }));
    }

    // Registrar provedor OAuth2
    registerProvider(name, config) {
        const strategy = new OAuth2Strategy({
            authorizationURL: config.authorizationURL,
            tokenURL: config.tokenURL,
            clientID: config.clientID,
            clientSecret: config.clientSecret,
            callbackURL: config.callbackURL,
            scope: config.scope || [],
            state: true // CSRF protection
        }, async (accessToken, refreshToken, profile, done) => {
            try {
                const user = await this.handleOAuthCallback(name, profile, accessToken);
                return done(null, user);
            } catch (error) {
                return done(error, null);
            }
        });

        passport.use(name, strategy);
        this.providers.set(name, { strategy, config });
    }

    // Handler de callback OAuth2
    async handleOAuthCallback(providerName, profile, accessToken) {
        // Validação do estado (CSRF protection)
        if (!this.validateState(profile.state)) {
            throw new Error('Invalid state parameter');
        }

        // Buscar ou criar usuário
        let user = await this.findUserByProviderId(providerName, profile.id);
        
        if (!user) {
            user = await this.createUserFromProfile(providerName, profile);
        }

        // Atualizar token de acesso
        await this.updateAccessToken(user.id, providerName, accessToken);

        // Gerar tokens JWT
        const tokens = await this.generateTokens(user);
        
        return {
            ...user,
            tokens
        };
    }

    // Gerar tokens JWT
    async generateTokens(user) {
        const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
        const secrets = securityConfig.generateSecrets();

        const accessToken = jwt.sign(
            {
                sub: user.id,
                email: user.email,
                roles: user.roles || ['user'],
                provider: user.provider
            },
            secrets.jwtSecret,
            {
                expiresIn: securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenExpiry,
                issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
                audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
            }
        );

        const refreshToken = crypto.randomBytes(40).toString('hex');
        
        // Armazenar refresh token com hash
        const hashedRefreshToken = crypto
            .createHash('sha256')
            .update(refreshToken)
            .digest('hex');

        await this.storeRefreshToken(user.id, hashedRefreshToken);

        return {
            accessToken,
            refreshToken,
            tokenType: 'Bearer',
            expiresIn: 900 // 15 minutos em segundos
        };
    }

    // Validação de estado (CSRF)
    validateState(state) {
        // Implementar validação de estado contra store
        return true; // Placeholder - implementar store real
    }

    // Métodos auxiliares (implementar com banco de dados real)
    async findUserById(id) {
        // Implementar busca no banco de dados
        return { id, email: 'user@example.com', roles: ['user'] };
    }

    async findUserByProviderId(provider, providerId) {
        // Implementar busca no banco de dados
        return null;
    }

    async createUserFromProfile(provider, profile) {
        // Implementar criação de usuário
        return {
            id: crypto.randomUUID(),
            email: profile.email,
            provider: provider,
            roles: ['user']
        };
    }

    async updateAccessToken(userId, provider, accessToken) {
        // Implementar atualização de token
    }

    async storeRefreshToken(userId, hashedToken) {
        // Implementar armazenamento seguro
    }

    async validateJwtPayload(payload) {
        // Implementar validação do payload JWT
        return { id: payload.sub, email: payload.email, roles: payload.roles };
    }
}

module.exports = new OAuth2Manager();
```

### 2.3 Estratégia Google OAuth2 (src/auth/strategies/googleStrategy.js)

```javascript
// src/auth/strategies/googleStrategy.js
const GoogleStrategy = require('passport-google-oauth20').Strategy;
const oauthManager = require('../oauth2');

const googleConfig = {
    clientID: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID,
    clientSecret: process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET,
    callbackURL: `${process.env.APP_URL}/auth/google/callback`,
    scope: ['profile', 'email'],
    state: true
};

// Registrar Google Strategy
oauthManager.registerProvider('google', {
    authorizationURL: 'https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/v2/auth',
    tokenURL: 'https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token',
    clientID: googleConfig.clientID,
    clientSecret: googleConfig.clientSecret,
    callbackURL: googleConfig.callbackURL,
    scope: googleConfig.scope
});

module.exports = {
    authenticate: () => {
        return oauthManager.passport.authenticate('google', {
            scope: googleConfig.scope,
            accessType: 'offline',
            prompt: 'consent'
        });
    },
    
    callback: () => {
        return oauthManager.passport.authenticate('google', {
            failureRedirect: '/login',
            failureFlash: true
        });
    }
};
```

## 3. Sanitização de Inputs (src/utils/sanitization.js)

```javascript
// src/utils/sanitization.js
const xss = require('xss');
const validator = require('validator');
const { createCipheriv, createDecipheriv, randomBytes } = require('crypto');
const { securityConfig } = require('../config/security');

class SanitizationManager {
    constructor() {
        // Configuração XSS
        this.xssOptions = {
            whiteList: {
                a: ['href', 'title', 'target'],
                p: [],
                br: [],
                strong: [],
                em: [],
                ul: [],
                ol: [],
                li: [],
                h1: [], h2: [], h3: [], h4: [], h5: [], h6: []
            },
            stripIgnoreTag: true,
            stripIgnoreTagBody: ['script', 'style', 'iframe']
        };

        this.xssFilter = new xss.FilterXSS(this.xssOptions);
    }

    // Sanitização de strings
    sanitizeString(input, options = {}) {
        if (!input || typeof input !== 'string') return '';

        let sanitized = input;
        
        // Trim
        sanitized = sanitized.trim();
        
        // Remove null bytes
        sanitized = sanitized.replace(/\0/g, '');
        
        // XSS Protection
        sanitized = this.xssFilter.process(sanitized);
        
        // SQL Injection Protection
        if (options.preventSQL) {
            sanitized = this.escapeSQL(sanitized);
        }
        
        // Max length
        if (options.maxLength && sanitized.length > options.maxLength) {
            sanitized = sanitized.substring(0, options.maxLength);
        }
        
        return sanitized;
    }

    // Escape para SQL
    escapeSQL(input) {
        if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
        
        return input
            .replace(/'/g, "''")
            .replace(/\\/g, '\\\\')
            .replace(/\0/g, '\\0')
            .replace(/\n/g, '\\n')
            .replace(/\r/g, '\\r')
            .replace(/\x1a/g, '\\Z');
    }

    // Validação de email
    validateEmail(email) {
        if (!email || typeof email !== 'string') return false;
        
        const sanitizedEmail = this.sanitizeString(email);
        return validator.isEmail(sanitizedEmail) && 
               sanitizedEmail.length <= 254;
    }

    // Validação de senha
    validatePassword(password) {
        if (!password || typeof password !== 'string') return false;
        
        // Mínimo 8 caracteres
        if (password.length < 8) return false;
        
        // Pelo menos uma letra maiúscula
        if (!/[A-Z]/.test(password)) return false;
        
        // Pelo menos uma letra minúscula
        if (!/[a-z]/.test(password)) return false;
        
        // Pelo menos um número
        if (!/\d/.test(password)) return false;
        
        // Pelo menos um caractere especial
        if (!/[!@#$%^&*(),.?":{}|<>]/.test(password)) return false;
        
        return true;
    }

    // Sanitização de objetos
    sanitizeObject(obj, schema) {
        if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return {};
        
        const sanitized = {};
        
        for (const [key, rules] of Object.entries(schema)) {
            if (obj.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                const value = obj[key];
                
                // Aplicar regras de sanitização
                if (rules.type === 'string') {
                    sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeString(value, rules.options || {});
                } else if (rules.type === 'email') {
                    sanitized[key] = this.validateEmail(value) ? this.sanitizeString(value) : null;
                } else if (rules.type === 'number') {
                    sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeNumber(value, rules.options || {});
                } else if (rules.type === 'boolean') {
                    sanitized[key] = Boolean(value);
                } else if (rules.type === 'array') {
                    sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeArray(value, rules.itemSchema);
                } else if (rules.type === 'object') {
                    sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeObject(value, rules.schema);
                }
            }
        }
        
        return sanitized;
    }

    // Sanitização de números
    sanitizeNumber(input, options = {}) {
        let num = Number(input);
        
        if (isNaN(num)) {
            return options.default || 0;
        }
        
        if (options.min !== undefined && num < options.min) {
            num = options.min;
        }
        
        if (options.max !== undefined && num > options.max) {
            num = options.max;
        }
        
        if (options.integer) {
            num = Math.round(num);
        }
        
        return num;
    }

    // Sanitização de arrays
    sanitizeArray(arr, itemSchema) {
        if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return [];
        
        return arr.map(item => {
            if (itemSchema.type === 'string') {
                return this.sanitizeString(item, itemSchema.options || {});
            } else if (itemSchema.type === 'object') {
                return this.sanitizeObject(item, itemSchema.schema);
            }
            return item;
        }).filter(item => item !== null && item !== undefined);
    }

    // Criptografia de dados sensíveis
    encryptSensitiveData(data, key = null) {
        const encryptionKey = key || securityConfig.generateSecrets().encryptionKey;
        const iv = randomBytes(securityConfig.encryption.ivLength);
        
        const cipher = createCipheriv(
            securityConfig.encryption.algorithm,
            encryptionKey,
            iv
        );
        
        let encrypted = cipher.update(data, 'utf8', 'hex');
        encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
        
        const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
        
        return {
            encrypted,
            iv: iv.toString('hex'),
            authTag: authTag.toString('hex'),
            algorithm: securityConfig.encryption.algorithm
        };
    }

    // Descriptografia de dados sensíveis
    decryptSensitiveData(encryptedData, key = null) {
        const encryptionKey = key || securityConfig.generateSecrets().encryptionKey;
        
        const decipher = createDecipheriv(
            encryptedData.algorithm,
            encryptionKey,
            Buffer.from(encryptedData.iv, 'hex')
        );
        
        decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(encryptedData.authTag, 'hex'));
        
        let decrypted = decipher.update(encryptedData.encrypted,

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]

class AIOpsDashboard {

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Plano de Testes

## 1. ESTRUTURA DE PASTAS DE TESTES

```
tests/
├── e2e/
│   ├── cypress/
│   │   ├── fixtures/
│   │   ├── integration/
│   │   │   ├── 01-authentication/
│   │   │   ├── 02-agent-management/
│   │   │   ├── 03-workflow-execution/
│   │   │   ├── 04-llm-integration/
│   │   │   └── 05-monitoring/
│   │   ├── plugins/
│   │   ├── support/

│   └── playwright/ (backup)
├── load/
│   ├── k6/
│   │   ├── smoke.js
│   │   ├── average-load.js

│   │   └── environments/
